### [1] [Scaling Generative Foundation Models for Chest Radiography with Rectified Flow Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19460)
*Fabio De Sousa Ribeiro,Emma A. M. Stanley,Charles Jones,Tian Xia,Dominic C. Marshall,Laurent Renard Triché,Christopher V. Cosgriff,Panagiotis Dimitrakopoulos,Sotirios A. Tsaftaris,Ben Glocker*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个从零开始训练的、参数量达十亿级的胸部X光片生成基础模型，旨在解决现有放射影像AI模型在不同患者群体、医疗机构和采集条件下的泛化能力差的问题。该模型基于120万张经专家指导的多源异构数据进行训练，具备可控生成与编辑能力，支持多种人口统计学特征、拍摄视角及十余种病理情况。其生成图像质量达到临床专家难以区分真实与合成图像的程度，显著提升了放射影像合成的保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有放射影像人工智能模型在不同患者群体、医疗机构和采集设置下泛化能力差，限制了其在真实临床环境中的应用。为提升数据多样性并评估诊断模型的鲁棒性，需要高保真、可控的胸部X光片合成方法。

Method: 构建一个包含1.2M张胸部X光片和临床专家标注元数据的大型异构数据集，训练一个参数量超过13亿的专用生成基础模型，使用1.6万亿标记进行训练，并实现对生成图像的多维度控制（如性别、年龄、病灶类型、拍摄视角等）。

Result: 生成的胸部X光片在视觉保真度上可被临床专家视为真实图像，且在多个子群体和病理情况下均表现出优异的可控性和多样性，显著超越现有技术。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了大规模、高保真、可控的胸部X光片生成，为医学影像数据增强、模型鲁棒性评估和跨机构部署提供了强有力的技术支持。

Abstract: We introduce the first generative foundation model for chest radiograph synthesis trained from scratch at the billion-parameter scale. Existing radiographic AI models often suffer from poor generalisation across patient subpopulations, institutions, and acquisition settings, resulting in limited real-world clinical utility. Controlled, high-fidelity synthesis of chest radiographs is a promising path toward diversifying clinical datasets and evaluating the robustness of diagnostic models. Therefore, we present the largest specialist generative foundation model for chest radiographs to date, with over 1.3B parameters, trained for 1.6T tokens on a curated, heterogeneous dataset comprising 1.2M radiographs and clinical expert-guided metadata. Our model supports controllable radiograph generation and editing across multiple demographic subgroups, acquisition views, and a dozen pathologies. Moreover, we significantly advance the state of the art in radiograph synthesis fidelity, producing images that are indistinguishable from real radiographs to clinical experts.

</details>


### [2] [LEAP: Layer-skipping Efficiency via Adaptive Progression for Vision Transformer Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19483)
*Jiaqi Zhang,Ashton Lee,Anthony Wong,John Zou,Sami BuGhanem,Randall Balestriero*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LEAP训练课程，通过渐进式难度选择提升ViT特征蒸馏效率，显著加速收敛并减少计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决特征蒸馏中因学生模型容量有限导致的教师-学生差距问题，提升小模型在边缘部署中的表现。

Method: 设计层跳过效率与自适应进展的训练课程，利用教师中间特征图作为逐步增加难度的目标，使学生先建立基础表示再学习高层抽象。

Result: 在ImageNet-100上，蒸馏后的ViT-S达到90.1%准确率，相比基线提升12.24%；在ImageNet-1K上，实例检索任务在Oxford和Paris数据集分别提升3.84%和7.75%；同时节省25.1%训练FLOPs和21%训练时间。

Conclusion: LEAP训练课程有效缓解了特征蒸馏中的容量瓶颈，提升了小模型性能并降低了训练成本，适用于多种模型规模和数据集。

Abstract: Vision Foundation Models (VFMs) with Vision Transformer (ViT) backbones, such as DINOv2, have become essential for downstream tasks like object recognition and semantic segmentation. The immense computational requirements of backbones often necessitate distillation into smaller architectures for edge deployment. Feature-based knowledge distillation (KD) often suffers from the teacher-student gap; the student struggles to imitate teacher's complex feature map due to its limited capacity. To mitigate this bottleneck, we propose LEAP: Layer-skipping Efficiency via Adaptive Progression, a training curriculum for ViT feature-based knowledge distillation. By utilizing the teacher's intermediate feature maps as a sequence of progressively more difficult targets, our curriculum allows the student to build a foundational representation before tackling higher-level abstractions. Our results demonstrate that this paradigm significantly accelerates convergence through adaptive difficulty selection across various student model sizes and dataset scales. With our curriculum, the LEAP-distilled ViT-S achieves 90.1% accuracy on ImageNet-100, a +12.24% improvement compared with baseline. On ImageNet-1K, LEAP achieves +3.84% and +7.75% improvement for the instance retrieval task on the Oxford and Paris datasets, respectively. Furthermore, the curriculum enables 25.1% savings in training FLOPs and 21% savings in training time on ImageNet-100 by implementing early-stopping for teacher inference during the initial stages of training. Code is available at https://github.com/KevinZ0217/LEAP

</details>


### [3] [LooseControlVideo: Directorial Video Control using Spatial Blocking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19495)
*Shariq Farooq Bhat,Niloy J. Mitra,Kalyan Sunkavalli*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LooseControlVideo introduces a novel framework for 3D spatial control in text-to-video generation using sparse, oriented 3D boxes as layout proxies. It enables intuitive high-level control over multi-object scenes while preserving realistic dynamics and occlusions through fine-tuning a Wan 2.2 backbone on a DNOCS-annotated video dataset. The method supports localized refinements without disrupting global context and outperforms existing baselines in trajectory accuracy, motion consistency, and occlusion modeling.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing depth-conditioned models require dense, frame-accurate annotations which are labor-intensive for dynamic, deformable scenes. There is a need for a more efficient and intuitive way to control complex 3D layouts and motions in text-to-video generation.

Method: The framework uses sparse oriented 3D boxes as 'blocking' proxies to guide scene layout and trajectory. It fine-tunes the Wan 2.2 model on a dataset annotated with DNOCS (a novel encoding for 3D size, orientation, and depth-ordered occlusions). Localized refinements are supported via minimal adjustments to the 3D box inputs.

Result: LooseControlVideo achieves 1.2x to 3x lower Trajectory Error, 2x higher Rigid Motion Consistency, and 1.5x to 2x better Occlusion Accuracy compared to state-of-the-art layout-conditioned models across nuScenes, HO-3D, and BEHAVE benchmarks.

Conclusion: Oriented 3D primitives serve as effective geometric priors for complex, multi-agent video generation, enabling intuitive, expressive, and accurate control over dynamic scenes with minimal annotation effort.

Abstract: Precise 3D spatial orchestration in text-to-video generation remains a significant challenge, particularly for multi-object scenes where semantic layout and temporal dynamics are often entangled. While existing depth-conditioned models achieve good structural fidelity, they necessitate dense, frame-accurate guidance that is labor-intensive to author for dynamic events involving deformable objects. We present LooseControlVideo, a framework that enables intuitive and expressive control by using sparse, oriented 3D boxes as a "blocking" proxy. This allows users to author high-level layout and trajectory while leveraging a video generative model to generate realistic occlusions, dynamics and interactions. We achieve this by fine-tuning a Wan 2.2 backbone on a video dataset annotated with DNOCS, a novel encoding for 3D size, orientation and depth-ordered occlusions. Furthermore, our method allows for localized refinement, such as adjusting a jump trajectory or adding an interaction, with minimal disruption to the global scene context. Extensive evaluations on the nuScenes, HO-3D, and BEHAVE benchmarks demonstrate that LooseControlVideo significantly outperforms existing 2D-box and flow-based baselines. Our findings indicate a 1.2x to 3x improvement in Trajectory Error; 2x improvement in Rigid Motion Consistency; and a 1.5x to 2x increase in Occlusion Accuracy over current state-of-the-art layout-conditioned models, demonstrating that oriented 3D primitives provide good geometric prior for complex, multi-agent video authoring.

</details>


### [4] [ImageWAM: Do World Action Models Really Need Video Generation, or Just Image Editing?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19531)
*Yuyang Zhang,Wenyao Zhang,Zekun Qi,He Zhang,Haitao Lin,Jingbo Zhang,Yao Mu,Xiaokang Yang,Wenjun Zeng,Xin Jin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ImageWAM提出了一种无需视频生成的世界行动模型框架，利用预训练的图像编辑模型来实现机器人动作预测。相比视频生成，图像编辑更聚焦于动作相关的视觉变化，提供更合适的先验知识，并通过压缩的键值缓存（KV caches）作为世界-动作上下文，显著降低计算开销（FLOPs减少至1/6，延迟降至1/4），同时在模拟器和真实场景中均优于传统VLA基线和竞争性WAM方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视频的世界行动模型（WAMs）存在推理成本高、冗余信息建模以及长时序预测误差累积等问题，且视频生成并非必要；因此需要探索更高效、更精准的替代方案。

Method: ImageWAM采用预训练图像编辑模型进行去噪处理，提取其产生的键值缓存（KV caches）作为紧凑的世界-动作上下文，不显式生成目标帧，而是将这些缓存输入到流匹配动作专家中以进行动作预测。

Result: ImageWAM在多个模拟与真实世界实验中表现优于标准VLA基线和竞争性WAM模型，同时将计算量降低至1/6，延迟降低至1/4，注意力分析显示缓存聚焦于任务相关的变化区域。

Conclusion: 图像编辑可作为视频生成的有效替代，为世界行动建模提供更高效、更精准的路径，表明世界行动模型未必依赖视频生成。

Abstract: World Action Models (WAMs) commonly rely on video generation to bridge visual world modeling and robot control. However, video-based WAMs face three coupled limitations: dense multi-frame future tokens make inference costly, full video prediction spends capacity on action-irrelevant temporal and appearance details, and long-horizon future imagination may introduce errors that mislead action prediction. These issues raise a simple question: Does world action model really need video generation? We propose ImageWAM, a simple WAM framework that repurposes pretrained image editing models for robot action prediction. In contrast to video generation, image editing provides a better-matched prior: it only needs to model a target-frame transformation, focuses on action-relevant current-to-target visual differences, and grounds task instructions to localized visual changes through edit pretraining. In practice, ImageWAM does not decode the target frame at inference time; instead, it conditions a flow-matching action expert on the KV caches produced by image-editing denoising, using them as a compact world-action context. ImageWAM outperforms standard VLA baselines and matching competitive WAMs without additional policy pretraining across different simulator and real-world experiments. It also reduces FLOPs to 1/6 and latency to 1/4 of video-based WAMs. Attention analysis further shows that editing caches focus on task-relevant change regions, supporting image editing as an effective alternative to video-based world-action modeling.

</details>


### [5] [PerceptionDLM: Parallel Region Perception with Multimodal Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19534)
*Yueyi Sun,Yuhao Wang,Jason Li,Ye Tian,Tao Zhang,Jacky Mai,Yihan Wang,Haochen Wang,Jinbin Bai,Ling Yang,Yunhai Tong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PerceptionDLM，一种基于扩散语言模型的多模态模型，用于高效并行区域感知。通过引入高效提示和结构化注意力掩码，实现多个区域描述的并行生成，显著提升多区域感知任务的推理效率。构建ParaDLC-Bench基准测试以评估并行性，实验表明该模型在保持高质量描述的同时大幅加速推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型依赖自回归生成，处理多个视觉区域时效率低下，难以满足高效并行感知的需求。为提升多区域视觉理解的效率，需探索非自回归架构的优势。

Method: 基于PerceptionDLM-Base构建，采用扩散语言模型的并行解码特性，设计高效提示机制与结构化注意力掩码，支持序列级和标记级的并行区域描述生成。

Result: PerceptionDLM在多区域图像描述任务中保持了与现有方法相当的生成质量，同时在推理速度上实现显著提升，验证了扩散语言模型在并行视觉感知中的潜力。

Conclusion: 本工作首次实现了基于扩散语言模型的并行区域感知与描述生成，证明了其在高效多区域视觉理解方面的可行性与优越性，为未来多模态模型设计提供了新方向。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved remarkable progress in visual understanding tasks. However, most existing MLLMs rely on autoregressive generation, which limits their efficiency for perception tasks that require captioning multiple regions. In this work, we propose PerceptionDLM, a multimodal diffusion language model optimized for efficient parallel region perception. Built upon PerceptionDLM-Base, a strong foundational baseline that achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source diffusion MLLMs, our architecture fully leverages the parallel decoding nature of DLMs. Specifically, we introduce efficient prompting and structured attention masking to enable simultaneous perception of multiple masked regions, allowing the model to generate region descriptions in parallel at both the sequence and token levels. This design significantly improves inference efficiency compared with existing approaches that process regions sequentially. To systematically evaluate the parallelism property of visual perception capability for DLMs, we construct a new Parallel Detailed Localized Captioning Benchmark (ParaDLC-Bench) by scaling the DLC-Bench to include multiple region masks per image, enabling joint evaluation of both caption quality and inference efficiency. Experiments demonstrate that PerceptionDLM maintains competitive performance in region captioning while achieving substantial speed improvements for multi-region perception tasks. Our results highlight the potential of multimodal diffusion language models for efficient, parallel visual perception. To the best of our knowledge, we are the first to achieve parallel region caption and perception by leveraging the advantages of diffusion language models. Code, models, and datasets are released.

</details>


### [6] [Mix-QVLA: Task-Evidence-Aware Mixed-Precision Quantization of Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19565)
*Navin Ranjan,Andreas Savakis*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Mix-QVLA是一种任务证据感知的混合精度量化框架，通过评估量化前后任务相关证据的保留情况，实现对视觉语言动作（VLA）模型的高效低比特部署。它利用归一化梯度加权的任务证据图，结合证据质量与归属分布畸变来衡量量化带来的影响，并引入软瓶颈目标函数生成层级敏感度评分，同时捕捉任务执行过程中层重要性的动态变化，从而在模型大小和计算预算下优化比特分配。实验表明，该方法显著提升了VLA模型的精度-效率平衡，在LIBERO上将内存从15.4GB降至4.1GB，成功率保持在96.3%（接近BF16的97.1%），并实现1.52倍推理加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化方法通常忽略任务相关证据在关键功能边界上的保留情况，难以有效指导低比特部署中不同层的比特分配。尤其对于复杂视觉语言动作（VLA）模型，其决策依赖于多阶段、跨模态的证据整合，固定敏感度假设导致资源分配不合理，限制了精度与效率的平衡。因此，亟需一种能感知任务证据变化、动态捕捉层重要性演化的混合精度量化框架。

Method: 提出Mix-QVLA框架，基于全精度动作令牌参考决策，计算各功能边界处的归一化梯度加权任务证据图；通过比较全精度与量化后证据图的证据质量（evidence-mass）与归属分布畸变（attribution-distribution distortion），量化量化带来的信息损失；设计软瓶颈目标函数，聚合边界级退化为层级敏感度评分；进一步建模任务执行过程中的相位依赖性，获取时间动态的敏感度变化；最终依据模型规模与BitOps预算，利用上述证据与时间感知得分进行混合精度比特分配。

Result: 在OpenVLA风格策略上广泛验证，结果表明Mix-QVLA显著改善了低比特部署下的精度-效率权衡。在LIBERO基准上，内存从15.4GB降低至4.1GB，平均成功率保持在96.3%（对比BF16模型的97.1%），实现1.52倍推理速度提升，证明其在压缩率、性能保持与推理效率方面的优越性。

Conclusion: Mix-QVLA通过任务证据感知与时间动态敏感度建模，实现了对复杂VLA模型更精准的混合精度量化。该方法不仅有效保留了关键决策证据，还实现了资源的智能分配，为低比特、高效率的VLA部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: We propose Mix-QVLA, a task-evidence-aware mixed-precision PTQ framework for VLA models. Mix-QVLA anchors each quantized variant to the full-precision action-token reference decision and evaluates whether quantization preserves task-relevant evidence across key VLA functional boundaries. It computes normalized gradient-weighted task-evidence maps from boundary activations and compares full-precision and quantized maps using evidence-mass and attribution-distribution distortion, capturing changes in both the strength and allocation of decision-supporting evidence. A soft-bottleneck objective aggregates boundary-level degradation into layer-wise sensitivity scores. Mix-QVLA further models sensitivity throughout task execution, capturing phase-dependent shifts in layer importance rather than assuming a fixed sensitivity profile. The resulting evidence- and time-aware scores guide mixed-precision bit allocation under model-size and BitOps budgets. Extensive evaluations on OpenVLA-style policies show that Mix-QVLA improves the accuracy-efficiency trade-off of low-bit VLA deployment. On LIBERO, Mix-QVLA reduces OpenVLA-OFT memory from 15.4 GB to 4.1 GB, retains 96.3 average success compared with 97.1 for the BF16 model, and achieves a 1.52x inference speedup.

</details>


### [7] [Language-Instructed Vision Embeddings for Controllable and Generalizable Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19584)
*Chengzhi Mao,Xudong Lin,Wen-Sheng Chu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种新方法LIVE，利用语言作为高阶指导，在推理时动态生成任务相关的视觉嵌入，无需任务特定的再训练，显著减少视觉幻觉，提升视觉问答性能，并能泛化到未见过的任务和指令。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉基础模型作为静态特征提取器，依赖大型下游模型进行任务适应，存在灵活性差、泛化能力有限的问题。需要一种更灵活、可适应的任务驱动视觉智能方法。

Method: 使用语言作为高阶指导，动态引导视觉编码器在推理时生成任务相关的视觉嵌入，实现无需再训练的任务自适应。

Result: 在MMVP上减少34点视觉幻觉；在视觉问答任务上超越参数量大得多的视觉语言模型；能够泛化到未见过的指令和任务。

Conclusion: LIVE提供了一条直接通向可适应、指令驱动的视觉智能的道路，实现了更可控、更具通用性的视觉表示。

Abstract: Vision foundation models are typically trained as static feature extractors, placing the burden of task adaptation onto large downstream models. We propose an alternative paradigm: instead of solely feeding visual features into language models, we use language itself to dynamically guide the vision encoder. Our method, Language-Instructed Vision Embeddings (LIVE), leverages language as high-level guidance to produce task-centric embeddings at inference time, removing the need for task-specific retraining. This enables the encoder to focus on contextually relevant aspects of the input, yielding more controllable and generalizable representations. Empirically, LIVE reduces visual hallucinations (+34 points on MMVP), surpasses vision-language models with orders of magnitude more parameters on visual question answering, and generalizes to unseen instructions and tasks -- offering a direct path toward adaptive, instruction-driven visual intelligence.

</details>


### [8] [GB-LSR: A Fast Local Spectral Image Representation with a Single Global Bandwidth for Continuous Reconstruction and Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19617)
*Max Shad,Naeem Khoshnevis*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GB-LSR提出一种固定网格的局部谱表示方法，用于连续图像重建。图像被划分为非重叠的方形块，每个块使用共享卷积编码器特征预测截断傅里叶基系数，全局共享一个可训练标量带宽，使得任意连续坐标上的重建成本与图像大小无关。在Kodak、Set14和Urban100基准上，主模型相比匹配预算的LIIF/LTE/WIRE实现，在PSNR上提升2.8-3.6 dB，LPIPS降低0.11-0.15，推理成本仅为最慢基线的四分之一。全局标量带宽已足够，局部自适应带宽未带来提升。在任意尺度超分辨率（ASR）扩展中，GB-LSR在标准协议下表现良好，速度比LIIF-RDN快1.44倍，比LTE-SwinIR快3.25倍；通过移除4角局部集成平均，速度提升1.77倍，峰值内存降低35%，且PSNR几乎不变；进一步扩大编码器通道数至96，带来轻微PSNR提升，速度加快1.58倍，内存降低31%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在图像重建中存在计算成本随图像尺寸增长的问题，且局部谱表示缺乏高效统一的带宽控制机制。本文旨在设计一种高效、可扩展的连续图像重建框架，实现低延迟、高精度重建，并支持任意尺度超分辨率。

Method: 将图像划分为非重叠方形块，利用共享卷积编码器提取特征并预测各块的截断傅里叶系数；采用全局共享的可训练标量带宽，实现固定大小基函数收缩，保证重建计算成本独立于图像尺寸；对比了全局标量、固定标量及每块自适应带宽三种变体，并在本地性诊断和端到端评估中验证其有效性。

Result: 在标准重建基准上，主模型优于匹配预算的LIIF/LTE/WIRE实现，PSNR提升2.8-3.6 dB，LPIPS降低0.11-0.15，推理成本仅为最慢基线的1/4；全局标量带宽已足够，无需每块自适应；在ASR任务中，速度显著提升，同时内存占用大幅下降，性能保持稳定或略有提升。

Conclusion: GB-LSR通过全局共享带宽与固定网格局部谱表示，实现了高效、高精度的连续图像重建与任意尺度超分辨率，具备优异的计算效率和可扩展性，为实际部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We present GB-LSR (Global-Bandwidth Local Spectral Representation), a fixed-grid local spectral representation for continuous image reconstruction. The image domain is partitioned into non-overlapping square patches, each carrying coefficients for a truncated Fourier basis predicted from shared convolutional-encoder features. A single trainable scalar bandwidth is shared globally across all patches and images, and reconstruction at any continuous coordinate is a fixed-size basis contraction whose cost is independent of image size. We study three bandwidth-handling variants: a trainable global scalar (main), a fixed global scalar, and a per-patch bandwidth field. On a standardized native-reconstruction benchmark across Kodak, Set14, and Urban100, the main variant outperforms matched-budget amortized LIIF / LTE / WIRE re-implementations by 2.8-3.6 dB PSNR and 0.11-0.15 LPIPS, while running at roughly one-quarter of the slowest baseline's inference cost. The single global scalar suffices empirically: per-patch adaptive-bandwidth alternatives do not improve over it on either a closed-form locality diagnostic or an end-to-end ablation. In a separate arbitrary-scale super-resolution (ASR) extension, GB-LSR achieves competitive PSNR-Y under a canonical-style SR protocol and runs 1.44x faster than LIIF-RDN and 3.25x faster than LTE-SwinIR at x4; within the same extension, a variant trained and evaluated without 4-corner local-ensemble averaging gives a 1.77x speedup with 35% lower peak memory and negligible PSNR change, while additionally widening the RDN encoder from 64 to 96 channels gives a small positive PSNR shift with a 1.58x speedup and 31% lower peak memory. Native-reconstruction claims are scoped to the matched-budget amortized protocol, and ASR claims are scoped to a separate canonical-style SR protocol.

</details>


### [9] [Learning When to Denoise: Optimizing Asynchronous Schedules for Latent Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19662)
*Bingshuo Qian,Xiang Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种学习异步调度的多表示扩散模型，通过构建可学习的凸单调参数化调度，在仅增加不到1%训练开销的情况下显著提升图像合成的收敛速度与最终质量。在ImageNet 256x256上，200轮训练即达到FID 1.05（匹配800轮SFD-XL），600轮时降至FID 1.02，优于更大模型的SFD-XXL结果。无引导设置下也表现优异，证明该方法高效且强大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多表示扩散模型依赖人工设计的异步调度，其性能受限于调度质量；而手动调优成本高、难以泛化。因此亟需一种可学习、自适应的调度机制以提升生成质量和训练效率。

Method: 提出基于多表示空间的异步流匹配框架，采用构造上为凸且单调的参数化调度函数，并引入调度修正目标以保持各表示局部加噪时间权重不变；通过快速联合探测器实现高效端到端学习，训练开销增加不足1%。

Result: 在ImageNet 256x256上，200轮训练模型达到FID 1.05，4倍减少训练量即达原800轮基线水平；600轮时FID降至1.02，优于1B参数的SFD-XXL（FID 1.04）。无引导设置下，200轮达FID 2.37，优于800轮基线（2.54），600轮进一步优化至2.14。

Conclusion: 所提可学习异步调度机制有效提升了多表示扩散模型的生成性能与训练效率，实现了更少训练轮次、更小模型规模下的高质量图像合成，具备显著实用价值。

Abstract: Multi-representation diffusion models can improve visual synthesis by denoising complementary views of an image, but their performance depends critically on the asynchronous schedule that determines when each representation is denoised. We propose to learn this schedule. Our method formulates asynchronous flow matching over multiple representation spaces and uses a schedule-corrected objective that keeps each representation's local noising-time weights fixed as the schedule changes. We instantiate the schedule with a flexible parametric class that is convex and monotone by construction, and learn it using a fast joint probe with less than 1% additional training compute. On ImageNet 256x256, the learned schedule substantially improves both convergence speed and final quality under a matched 675M-parameter XL backbone. With AutoGuidance, our 200-epoch model reaches FID 1.05, matching the 800-epoch SFD-XL baseline with 4x less training. Training to 600 epochs further improves to FID 1.02, outperforming the 1B-parameter SFD-XXL result of FID 1.04 while using a smaller model. In the unguided setting, our 200-epoch model reaches FID 2.37, already below the best 800-epoch SFD-XL result (2.54) at 4x less training, and improves to FID 2.14 at 600 epochs. Code is available at https://github.com/bsq532087/LWD

### [10] [TeleMorpher: Toward Robust Simultaneous Motion-Location Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19676)
*Haengbok Chung*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TeleMorpher 是首个已知的一次性框架，用于同时进行运动和位置编辑。它通过利用运动先验、目标运动中心的视频作为编辑引导，并结合真实运动信息，实现更可控、精确的编辑。方法包括：1）使用预训练分割与修复模型分离主角与背景；2）引入无需训练的姿态扭曲来以运动先验为指导编辑主角动作；3）将扭曲后的动作视频直接注入基线动作编辑器中，减少源与目标动作差异并保留源视频外观；4）提出两种基于LPIPS的新指标，评估背景一致性和动作编辑保真度。实验表明，TeleMorpher在真实人类评价和定量指标上均表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散模型在图像和视频生成中取得显著进展，但对运动与位置的联合编辑仍缺乏有效方法。尽管运动编辑已有研究，但同时改变动作和位置的编辑尚未被充分探索，尤其在保持视觉一致性方面存在挑战。因此，需要一种能同时控制运动与位置变化且保持高质量输出的方法。

Method: 1. 使用预训练分割与修复模型分离主角与背景；2. 提出无需训练的姿态扭曲模块，以运动先验为引导修改主角动作；3. 将处理后的动作视频注入基线运动编辑器，以减小源与目标动作差异并保持源视频外观；4. 设计两个基于LPIPS的评估指标，分别衡量背景一致性和动作骨架保真度。

Result: 在真实世界视频和太极数据集上的实验显示，TeleMorpher 在定量和定性评估中均优于现有方法，尤其在人类主观评价中表现突出，验证了其在运动-位置联合编辑中的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: TeleMorpher 作为首个一次性的运动-位置联合编辑框架，通过融合运动先验与结构化编辑策略，在保持外观一致性和动作自然性方面表现出色，为未来视频编辑提供了新思路。

Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in image and video generation and editing. While recent studies have extended these efforts toward motion editing, simultaneously transforming both motion and location-despite its practical importance-remains largely unexplored. To better understand robust motion-location editing, we first analyze the fundamental factors that degrade its quality. Based on this analysis, we propose TeleMorpher, one of the first one-shot frameworks to the best of our knowledge, for simultaneous motion-location editing. Our approach leverages motion priors, a target motion-centric video generated from an off-the-shelf model as motion-editing guidance, and the ground truth motion to enable more controllable and precise motion-location editing. Via this, our framework works as follows: (1) we first disentangle the protagonist and the background via pre-trained segmentation and inpainting models. (2) Then, we introduce a training-free pose warping that edits the protagonist's motion with the motion prior as the guidance. (3) The result of warped motion video is directly injected into a baseline motion editor during inference, mitigating the difference between source and target motions while preserving the appearance of the source video. (4) To enhance the reliability of quantitative evaluations, we propose two new LPIPS-based metrics that measure the background consistency before and after the motion editing and the fidelity of motion editing performance via measuring the difference between the extracted protagonist's skeletons from source and target videos. Experiments with in-the-wild videos and the TaiChi dataset demonstrate that TeleMorpher achieves superior performance across both quantitative and qualitative measurements (real-human evaluation), underscoring its effectiveness.

To enhance interactivity, Vortex incorporates Rocchio-based relevance feedback and a multi-stage temporal search mechanism for sequential event alignment. ### [13] [NEST: Narrative Event Structures in Time for Long Video Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19706)
*Ali Asgarov,Kaushik Narasimhan,Najibul Haque Sarker,Hani Alomari,Chia-Wei Tang,Anushka Sivakumar,Zaber Ibn Abdul Hakim,Shaurya Mallampati,Chris Thomas*

Abstract: Recent progress in vision-language models has enabled the processing of increasingly long video sequences, but the ability to handle extended token streams does not translate to understanding of narrative structure in long videos. Existing long video benchmarks focus on needle-in-a-haystack retrieval rather than evaluating how low-level actions form events, how events interact across time, and how narratives progress, for example, whether a model can connect an early setback, such as a job loss to a later relationship breakup, despite long gaps, intervening scenes, or flashbacks that reframe what occurred. We introduce NEST (Narrative Event Structures in Time for Long Video Understanding), a dataset of 1005 full-length movies (avg. 98 minutes), each annotated with 102 multimodal narrative events grounded in visual content, dialogue, and audio. NEST captures multimodal narrative events with structured annotations grounded in visual content, dialogue, and audio, and links them through relations that reflect narrative structure, including temporal ordering, hierarchical composition, and long-range dependencies. We introduce baselines for event trigger detection (ETD), event localization (EL), event argument extraction (EAE), and event relation extraction (ERE). The benchmark is highly challenging for grounded event discovery, with ETD below 8%, EL under 6%, and EAE below 11%. In contrast, ERE is more tractable once events are given, reaching 35.45% F1 zero-shot and 44.42% F1 after fine-tuning.

### [14] [One-Shot Novel View and Pose Human Image Synthesis via 3D Prior Guided Diffusion Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19718)
*Shenjian Gong,Kangkan Wang,Shanshan Zhang,Jian Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于条件去噪扩散模型的单图像新视角与新姿态人体图像合成方法，通过引入3D人体先验（如3D法线图和颜色提示）作为几何与颜色条件，解决现有方法在复杂姿态下无法准确处理遮挡或不可见部位的问题。该方法通过一系列扩散步骤实现高质量人体生成，并采用自重构定制化精修策略增强细节表现。实验表明，该方法在多个公开数据集上显著优于先前方法，具备更强的泛化能力。

Abstract: This paper addresses the challenge of one-shot novel view and pose human image synthesis. The existing methods transfer the reference human image to a target pose using a set of 2D pose keypoints or synthesize human images based on generalizable human NeRF which uses human model priors to extract point-wise features. However, pose transfer based methods can not handle complex human pose using ambiguous 2D pose as the condition, while generalizable human NeRFs may be inaccurate to recover occluded/invisiable human parts without extracted reliable features. To solve these problems, we propose a novel approach for novel view and pose synthesis from a singe human image via conditional denoising diffusion model. Our diffusion model divides the novel view and pose synthesis problem into a sequence of conditional denoising steps. Specifically, to generate humans with complex and arbitrary poses, we introduce 3D human priors, i.e., 3D normal map and color prompt, as geometry and color conditions into the generation process. By transferring the reference human into the target human with a series of diffusion steps, our diffusion model enables high-quality synthesis including the occluded/invisible parts. Further, we propose a self-reconstruction based customized refinement to enhance fine details when tested on novel persons.Experimental results on different public datasets demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms previous methods and also shows better generalization ability across datasets. The code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/Yankeegsj/3DPGDM.

### [15] [QueryGaussian: Scalable and Training-Free Open-Vocabulary 3D Instance Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19733)
*Xiuyuan Zhu,Ke Lu,Zijie Yang,Chao Yue,Jian Xue,Dongming Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: QueryGaussian 是一种无需训练的高效、可扩展的开放词汇3D实例检索框架，通过实例级查询机制避免了传统方法中因场景复杂度增加导致的内存与计算开销线性增长问题。它利用预训练2D视觉模型理解自然语言提示，并通过最大权重关联策略将分割掩码映射到3D空间，结合时间融合模块与多阶段自适应密度聚类缓解投影模糊问题。实验表明，该方法在保持先进精度的同时，显著降低GPU内存使用超过70%，推理速度提升180倍，可在消费级硬件上实现包含数千万高斯点的城市级场景快速检索。

Motivation: 现有3D实例检索方法依赖于‘场景级嵌入’范式，需对每个3D原始体进行高维语义特征压缩，导致内存和计算成本随场景复杂度线性上升，在城市规模场景中极易引发内存溢出（OOM）问题，亟需更高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Method: 提出QueryGaussian框架，采用实例级查询机制，分离语义理解与几何表示；利用预训练2D视觉模型解析用户自然语言提示，生成对应分割掩码并映射至3D空间；通过并发最大权重关联策略保证语义-视觉一致性；引入时间融合模块与多阶段自适应密度聚类以缓解投影模糊。

Result: QueryGaussian在保持与最先进方法相当的准确率基础上，实现超过70%的GPU内存节省和180倍的推理加速，成功支持在消费级硬件上对包含数千万高斯点的城市级大规模场景进行快速实例检索。

Conclusion: QueryGaussian通过解耦语义与几何表示，突破了传统方法在大规模3D场景中的效率瓶颈，为开放词汇3D实例检索提供了高效、可扩展的新范式，具备在真实世界大规模场景中落地应用的潜力。

Abstract: Efficiently retrieving specific 3D instances from large-scale scenes via natural language prompts remains a formidable challenge in multimedia analysis. Existing approaches predominantly follow a "scene-level embedding" paradigm, which requires distilling high-dimensional semantic features into every 3D primitive. This strategy suffers from a fundamental architectural bottleneck: memory and computational costs scale linearly with scene complexity, inevitably triggering out-of-memory (OOM) failures in city-scale environments. To address this barrier, we propose QueryGaussian, a training-free framework for expeditious and scalable open-vocabulary 3D instance retrieval. Unlike holistic semantic distillation, QueryGaussian employs an instance-level query mechanism that decouples semantic understanding from geometric representation. Specifically, we leverage pre-trained 2D vision models to interpret user prompts and lift segmentation masks into 3D via a concurrent maximum-weight association strategy, ensuring semantic-visual consistency. To mitigate projection ambiguity, we introduce a temporal fusion module with multi-stage adaptive density clustering. Experimental results demonstrate that QueryGaussian not only matches the accuracy of state-of-the-art methods but also delivers a decisive efficiency leap, reducing GPU memory usage by over 70% and accelerating inference by 180x. Crucially, QueryGaussian enables expeditious instance retrieval on city-scale scenes containing tens of millions of Gaussians using consumer-grade hardware.

Existing methods either optimize 2D digital perturbations that fail to generalize to dynamic viewpoints or produce visually unnatural textures that cannot be deployed in real scenarios. Therefore, we propose an end-to-end framework for adversarial camouflage generation that automatically produces wearable adversarial patterns and maintains stable attack performance in real physical environments with changing viewpoints, poses, and lighting conditions. Our method integrates UV-volume rendering with a diffusion-based texture generator, enabling consistent appearance under varying scales, poses, and lighting conditions. To ensure environmental realism, we propose an illumination color consistency estimator that extracts dominant background attributes and guides a natural texture loss to align the generated UV texture with the surrounding environment. Specifically, Occ-VLM reconstructs 3D scene occupancy as an auxiliary geometric prior, which is utilized to spatially associate foreground 2D tokens with 3D space. These tokens are then decoded by a Large Language Model (LLM) for unified scene understanding. ### [18] [HypOProto: Hyperbolic Ordinal Prototypes for Left Ventricular Filling Pressure Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19804)
*Victoria Wu,Nima Hashemi,Hooman Vaseli,Christina Luong,Purang Abolmaesumi,Teresa S. M. Tsang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HypOProto框架，利用双曲原型对心超声图像中的左心室充盈压（LVFP）进行可解释分类。该方法基于冻结的可解释基础模型，通过双曲空间中的序数原型排列，模拟临床生理学中的E/e'分级，提升分类性能与可解释性。引入新型双曲原型角度分离损失（HyperPAS），增强类别间原型区分度。在保持最先进性能的同时，实现透明化决策，并可视化关键临床区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习的LVFP分类方法虽性能优异，但多为黑箱模型，缺乏临床可解释性；且传统依赖操作者判断的E/e'比值在资源有限地区难以获取。因此亟需一种既准确又可解释、无需依赖人工测量的自动化方法。

Method: 提出一种双曲序数原型框架HypOProto，将原型按生理上合理的E/e'尺度分布于双曲空间中：边缘病例靠近双曲根部，正常与异常病例分布在外部以体现诊断确定性。采用冻结的基础模型提取特征，并结合新颖的HyperPAS损失函数，在双曲空间中强制类间原型分离。

Result: HypOProto在多个数据集上达到当前最优性能，同时显著提升模型可解释性；可视化结果能清晰指出与诊断相关的图像区域，符合临床逻辑。

Conclusion: HypOProto是首个用于心超图像中LVFP分类的原型驱动框架，融合双曲几何建模与可解释性设计，实现了高性能与临床透明性的统一，为未来智能医疗系统提供新范式。

Abstract: Echocardiography (echo) is a widely used imaging modality for assessing cardiac function, with Left Ventricular Filling Pressure (LVFP) serving as a critical physiological marker for conditions such as heart failure. Standard LVFP classification into normal \emph{vs} elevated categories relies on the Doppler-derived $E/e'$ ratio, which is operator-dependent and often unavailable in resource-limited settings, motivating methods that infer LVFP directly from B-mode echo. Existing deep learning approaches achieve high performance but remain largely black-box, limiting clinical interpretability. We propose HypOProto, a hyperbolic, ordinal prototype-based framework for interpretable LVFP classification using a frozen, explainable foundation model backbone. HypOProto arranges prototypes along the physiological $E/e'$ scale, placing borderline cases near the hyperboloid root where small angular differences separate similar cases, while normal and elevated cases occupy outward positions reflecting increasing diagnostic certainty. This hyperbolic geometry encodes clinically meaningful ordinal relationships and improves interpretability. We also introduce a novel Hyperbolic Prototype Angular Separation (HyperPAS) loss, enforcing inter-class prototype separation in hyperbolic space. HypOProto achieves SOTA performance while maintaining transparency, and highlights clinically relevant regions in visualizations. This work represents the first prototype-based framework for LVFP classification in echo. Our code can be found at https://github.com/DeepRCL/HypOProto.

### [19] [ParaScale: Scale-Calibrated Camera-Motion Transfer via a Gauge-Invariant Parallax Number](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19805)
*Zijie Meng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出ParaScale方法，通过引入无量纲的几何不变量——视差数Pi（Parallax Number Pi），解决参考视频与目标视频间尺度不匹配导致的相机运动转移失真问题。Pi = ||ΔT|| / Z̄，衡量相机移动在图像中产生的感知强度，其值不受深度尺度影响。论文设计了一种无需重新训练的插件式模块，在姿态提取与注入之间动态调整参考轨迹，使目标场景中的运动感知与原参考一致。同时引入尺度对称的评估指标PCE（Parallax Consistency Error），比传统指标更敏感地揭示尺度错配问题。实验表明，ParaScale在跨越四个数量级的尺度下均显著降低PCE（超3倍），且保持视觉质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当将参考视频的相机运动迁移到新生成视频时，由于参考与目标场景尺度差异大（如星系扫动与桌面微移），直接复用原始运动轨迹会导致运动过弱或过强，无法真实再现原有意图。现有方法缺乏对运动感知尺度的建模，导致转移结果失真。

Method: 提出视差数Pi作为度量相机运动感知强度的无量纲、几何不变量；设计ParaScale模块，在姿态注入前根据目标场景深度动态缩放参考轨迹，仅调整平移分量，保留旋转；引入新的尺度对称评估指标PCE，用于量化尺度不匹配程度。

Result: ParaScale在多种模型和尺度条件下，使实际实现的视差与理想值保持一致（落在身份线），相比未校准的转移方式，PCE下降超过3倍，且视觉保真度无损失。

Conclusion: 通过引入视差数Pi和对应的ParaScale模块，实现了尺度忠实的相机运动迁移。该方法具有通用性、无需重训练，能有效解决跨尺度运动转移中的感知失真问题，为视频生成中的镜头语言复用提供了可靠基础。

Abstract: Transferring the camera motion of a reference video to a freshly generated one lets creators reuse cinematic moves. Yet reference and target often live at incompatible scales -- a sweep across a galaxy versus a nudge across a desk -- and naively reusing the recovered trajectory yields either imperceptible or violently exaggerated motion. We trace this to a geometric fact: translation-induced image motion scales as ||T||/Z, so a monocular trajectory is meaningful only up to a depth-scale gauge. We distill this into the Parallax Number Pi = ||Delta T|| / Zbar, a dimensionless, gauge-invariant descriptor of how strongly a camera move is felt, and prove that it -- not the raw trajectory -- is the quantity that scale-faithful transfer must preserve. ParaScale is a plug-and-play module that reads Pi off any reference video and re-realizes it against the target scene's own depth, per frame, leaving rotation untouched. Sitting between pose extraction and pose injection, it requires no retraining and drops into any pose-conditioned generator. We further introduce the Parallax Consistency Error (PCE), a scale-symmetric metric that -- unlike the similarity-aligned TransErr -- exposes scene-scale mismatch. Across scale regimes spanning four orders of magnitude and multiple backbones, ParaScale keeps the realized parallax on the identity line and cuts PCE by more than 3x over uncalibrated transfer with no loss of visual fidelity.

</details>


### [20] [Training-Free Metrics for Synthetic Object Detection Data: A Proxy for Detector Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19817)
*Myeongseok Nam,Donghoon Yeo,Seungwook Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为条件-组合域匹配（CCDM）的预计算度量方法，用于评估合成数据集在目标检测任务中的相对有效性。该方法可避免反复训练下游模型以评估合成数据的效果，显著降低计算成本。在VisDrone-DET数据集上的实验表明，CCDM与YOLOv8的下游性能具有1.0的斯皮尔曼相关性，显著优于现有评估指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前图像生成模型催生了大量合成数据，但其对下游目标检测模型的提升效果差异大，而传统评估方式需反复训练模型，计算成本高且耗时，尤其在需要密集标注的检测任务中问题更突出。因此亟需一种高效、预计算的评估方法来筛选有效的合成数据集。

Method: 提出了一种名为条件-组合域匹配（CCDM）的度量方法，通过分析合成数据与真实数据在特征空间中的分布一致性，结合条件概率和组合结构，构建一个可预先计算的代理指标，用于预测合成数据集对下游检测模型的实用价值。

Result: 在VisDrone-DET数据集上，CCDM度量与YOLOv8的下游检测性能呈现1.0的斯皮尔曼相关性，证明其能精准反映合成数据集的有效性；同时显著优于现有合成图像评估指标。

Conclusion: CCDM作为一种高效的预计算指标，能够准确预测合成数据集在目标检测任务中的相对性能，为合成数据的选择提供了可靠、低成本的评估手段，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: With the recent advent of image generative models, synthetic data are increasingly being used to supplement limited real datasets for training computer vision models. However, not all synthetic datasets improve performance equally, and their effectiveness can only be assessed by training a downstream model, which is computationally expensive and time-consuming. This problem is pronounced in the task of object detection, where the required annotations are much more dense due to bounding boxes. In this paper, we propose a pre-computable metric family, dubbed Conditional-Composition Domain Match (CCDM), which serves as a proxy for the relative utility of candidate synthetic training sets for downstream detection. Experiments on the VisDrone-DET dataset show that the CCDM metric families achieve a Spearman correlation of 1.0 with the downstream performance of YOLOv8, clearly outperforming existing metrics for synthetic image evaluation.

*Junho Moon,Haejun Chung,Ikbeom Jang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CSWinUNETR是一种用于2D和3D细长结构分割的通用骨干网络，通过交叉条带自注意力、循环移位和细节增强的多尺度自注意力模块，有效建模长距离主轴上下文并保留细粒度细节。此外，引入稀疏控制动态蛇形卷积，从稀疏预测的控制点重建可靠的密集曲线核，以更好地遵循复杂几何形状。在眼科、神经血管成像和皮肤病学四个基准测试中，CSWinUNETR均优于现有方法，无需任务特定后处理或拓扑感知损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确分割低对比度、频繁断续且存在严重类别不平衡的细长解剖结构（如视网膜血管、脑血管和面部皱纹）仍具挑战性。现有卷积和基于Transformer的模型常产生碎片化预测，难以恢复细小分支。

Method: 提出CSWinUNETR，采用交叉条带自注意力建模长距离主轴上下文，利用循环移位增强条带间信息交换；引入细节增强的多尺度自注意力模块，聚合多分辨率特征；设计稀疏控制动态蛇形卷积，从稀疏控制点重建密集曲线核以适应弯曲结构。

Result: 在四个跨领域的基准测试中，包括眼科、神经血管成像和皮肤病学，CSWinUNETR consistently表现优于当前最优方法，无需任务特定后处理或拓扑感知损失，显著提升细长结构的连续性和完整性。

Conclusion: CSWinUNETR为2D和3D细长结构分割提供了一种高效、通用的解决方案，其设计有效应对了低对比度、断裂和几何复杂性等挑战，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Accurate segmentation of thin, tortuous anatomical structures, such as retinal vessels, cerebral vasculature, and facial wrinkles, remains challenging due to low contrast, frequent discontinuities, and severe class imbalance. Although recent convolutional and Transformer-based models have improved performance, they often yield fragmented predictions and fail to recover fine branches. We propose CSWinUNETR, a general-purpose backbone for 2D and 3D thin-structure segmentation. It employs cross-shaped stripe self-attention to model long-range principal-axis context and incorporates cyclic shifts to enhance information exchange across stripes. To better preserve fine-grained details, we further introduce a detail-enhanced multi-scale self-attention module that aggregates contextual features from multi-resolution representations. In addition, we propose sparse-control dynamic snake convolution, which reconstructs reliable dense curvilinear kernels from sparsely predicted control points to better follow tortuous geometry. Extensive experiments on four benchmarks across ophthalmology, neurovascular imaging, and dermatology demonstrate that CSWinUNETR consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods without task-specific post-processing or topology-aware losses. The code is available at https://github.com/labhai/CSWinUNETR.

### [22] [3D-PLOT-LLM: Part-Level Object Tokens for 3D Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19828)
*Jintang Xue,Xinyu Wang,Yixing Wu,Jingwen Chen,C. -C. Jay Kuo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 3D-PLOT-LLM 提出一种新方法，通过重新组织输入令牌流，使3D对象的各个部分可通过大语言模型的词汇直接引用。该模型将点编码器的补丁划分为K个局部连贯区域，并在每个区域前插入可学习的区域标记和保留词汇标记<part_k>，结合空间统计与邻接关系进行标记优化。此设计实现了对部件的命名、推理与引用能力，显著优于以往依赖分割解码器或边界框语法的方法。实验表明，其在PartVerse-QA和3DCoMPaT-GrIn等基准上表现优异，仅需不到100万新增参数，且无需额外解码器或边界框头，大幅降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D多模态大模型虽能整体描述3D对象，但无法有效识别、命名或推理其组成部分；传统方法通过增加分割解码器、更复杂的3D编码器或边界框语法提升部分感知能力，但带来巨大参数开销。因此亟需一种轻量级、高效且能直接利用大语言模型词汇进行部件操作的新范式。

Method: 将点云编码器输出的补丁划分为K个局部连通区域，在每个区域前插入可学习的区域标记和预留词汇标记<part_k>；引入标记-空间精炼（MSR）模块，基于区域的空间特征与邻接关系动态调整标记内容，使语言模型能够以词元形式引用特定部件。

Result: 在PartVerse-QA上达到0.459的caption-to-slots Jaccard分数和13.78%的精确匹配率，GPT-4o评分达44.68；在3DCoMPaT-GrIn上超越PointLLM、Kestrel、PARIS3D、SegPoint及ShapeLLM；在Objaverse全对象描述任务中，加入第二阶段训练后，性能超越PointLLM，优于PointLLM-PiSA在多数指标上。所有结果均仅使用不足100万新增参数，远低于此前方法。

Conclusion: 3D-PLOT-LLM 通过重构输入表示，实现轻量化、高效率的部件可访问性，首次在不增加复杂结构的前提下，使3D MLLM具备真正的部件命名与推理能力，为后续3D理解提供了全新路径。

Abstract: 3D multimodal large language models (3D MLLMs) describe a 3D object as a whole but cannot address, name, or reason about its parts. Prior part-aware attempts add segmentation decoders, heavier 3D encoders, or bounding-box grammars at substantial parameter cost. We take a fundamentally different path: we reorganize the input token stream so that parts become directly addressable through the LLM's own vocabulary. Our model, 3D-PLOT-LLM, partitions the frozen point encoder's patches into K locally coherent regions and inserts, before each region's patch tokens, a learnable per-region marker and a reserved vocabulary token <part_k>; a Marker-Space Refinement (MSR) module then conditions each marker on its region's spatial statistics and adjacency neighbors. The model thus cites parts in its output and follows prompts that refer to parts by token, a capability absent from prior object-level 3D MLLMs. To probe this interface, we construct PartVerse-QA, a vocabulary-level part-QA benchmark adapted from PartVerse mesh annotations (77K training pairs and 588 held-out queries on disjoint object splits), on which 3D-PLOT-LLM reaches caption-to-slots Jaccard 0.459 and Exact-match 13.78%, with a slot-to-caption GPT-4o judge of 44.68. On the 3DCoMPaT-GrIn part-aware grounded description benchmark, 3D-PLOT-LLM outperforms PointLLM, Kestrel, PARIS3D, and SegPoint on every text-output metric, and ShapeLLM on 3 of 4, with up to +3.03 GPT-4o judge over PointLLM. On Objaverse whole-object captioning, adding PartVerse-QA at Stage 2 yields +0.65 SBERT and +1.85 GPT-4o over PointLLM, and tops PointLLM-PiSA on 4 of 5 traditional metrics (SBERT, SimCSE, BLEU-1, METEOR) despite targeting a different (part-grounded) objective. All with under 1M new trainable parameters on a frozen point encoder, an order of magnitude below prior part-aware 3D MLLMs, and no segmentation decoder or bounding-box head.

</details>


### [23] [Neural Events: Discrete Asynchronous Autoencoders for Event-Based Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19835)
*Roberto Pellerito,Daniel Gehrig,Shintaro Shiba,Davide Scaramuzza*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种新框架，将事件流重新标记为少量高信息量的'神经事件'，每个神经事件代表一个局部时空上下文窗口，并以可学习的离散代码表示。当代码发生变化时触发神经事件，从而大幅压缩数据流。实验表明，在目标检测和分类任务中，基于神经事件的网络性能达到或超过现有最先进方法，同时事件率降低2倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事件相机系统产生的事件流数据量巨大且单个事件信息量低，导致下游算法难以高效处理，难以在捕捉精细时间动态和控制数据吞吐量之间取得平衡。

Method: 将原始事件流重新标记为由可学习离散代码表示的神经事件，通过代码变化触发事件，实现对事件流的高度压缩与语义增强。

Result: 在物体检测和分类任务中，使用神经事件训练的模型性能与现有最佳方法相当或更优，同时事件率降低2倍。

Conclusion: 该框架有效解决了事件流处理中的信息冗余与计算负担问题，实现了高性能与低数据率的兼顾。

Abstract: Event cameras capture dynamic scenes with exceptional temporal fidelity by representing them as a continuous stream of microsecond resolution \textit{events}. Each individual event, however, only carries minimal semantic value, merely signaling a localized brightness change. To derive meaningful signals, downstream algorithms need to quickly integrate cues from a potentially massive torrent of low-information events. Current architectures, however, are easily overwhelmed, struggling to balance capturing fine-grained temporal dynamics and maintaining a manageable data throughput. This paper proposes a framework to re-tokenize event streams into a small set of highly informative \textit{neural events}, each representing a local spatio-temporal context window with a discrete learnable code. Every time this code flips, a neural event is triggered, yielding a highly compressed data stream. We demonstrate that, across object detection and classification, networks trained on neural events are on par or surpass the performance of state-of-the-art approaches while reducing the event rate by a factor of 2.0.

### [24] [OTCHA: Optimal Transport-driven Confidence-aware Latent Hub Alignment for Multi-View Medical Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19838)
*Jiwoong Yang,Haejun Chung,Ikbeom Jang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OTCHA提出一种基于最优传输（OT）的置信度感知潜在枢纽令牌对齐模块，用于多视图医学图像分类。该方法通过共享的可学习潜在枢纽令牌，利用考虑特征相似性和几何结构的OT计划，对各视图的补丁令牌进行精炼，同时引入条件尘箱实现部分匹配并剔除无关令牌。最终通过令牌级匹配置信度控制消息传递和加权优化传输表示对齐损失，提升融合鲁棒性。在三个多视图医学图像数据集上实验表明，OTCHA在多种解剖结构和视图配置下均优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法直接融合各视图表示，导致视图特有伪影或无关背景信息污染融合嵌入，降低在不同视图配置下的鲁棒性。需要一种能有效去除无关内容、精准对齐关键特征的多视图融合机制。

Method: 提出OTCHA模块，包含可学习的跨视图共享潜在枢纽令牌；为每个视图计算基于特征相似性和几何结构的最优传输计划；引入令牌条件尘箱支持部分匹配与无关令牌剔除；利用传输计划生成的置信度门控枢纽消息传递，并设计基于最优传输的表示对齐损失以稳定特征精炼过程。

Result: 在三个多视图医学图像数据集上，OTCHA在不同解剖结构和视图配置下均实现一致性能提升，显著优于现有基线方法，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OTCHA通过引入置信度感知的最优传输对齐机制，有效解决了多视图医学图像中因视图特异性噪声和无关背景导致的融合偏差问题，提升了多视图分类的准确性与稳定性，具有良好的临床应用潜力。

Abstract: Multi-view imaging, such as mammography and chest radiography, is a standard component of clinical practice. However, medical images are often unregistered and contain view-specific artifacts or irrelevant background cues that can obscure diagnostically relevant findings. Many existing methods directly fuse per-view representations, allowing such irrelevant content to contaminate the fused embedding and reducing robustness under varying view configurations. We propose OTCHA, a confidence-aware latent hub token alignment module based on optimal transport (OT) that refines patch tokens before fusion for multi-view classification. OTCHA introduces a set of learnable latent hub tokens shared across views. For each view, we compute an OT plan between patch tokens and hub tokens that jointly considers feature similarity and geometry, and augment the OT formulation with token-conditional dustbins to enable partial matching and discard irrelevant tokens. The resulting transport plan provides token-wise matching confidence, which gates hub-mediated message passing and weights a novel optimal-transport-based representation alignment loss to stabilize refinement. Experiments on three multi-view medical image datasets demonstrate consistent improvements over competing baselines across diverse anatomies and view configurations. Our code is available at https://github.com/labhai/OTCHA.

Abstract: Streaming VideoLLMs must continuously process incoming video while maintaining low query latency, making both video-ingestion throughput and query-time responsiveness critical for real-time deployment. Existing methods largely focus on accelerating individual modules, such as visual encoding, token pruning, or KV-cache compression, but provide limited insight into whether the resulting system can sustain real-time streaming performance. We formulate streaming VideoLLM inference as a coordinated pipeline spanning visual preprocessing, visual encoding, token dropping, and LLM prefilling/decoding. Building on this formulation, we propose ViCoStream (Video Coordinated Streaming), a stage-wise coordinated streaming framework that combines chunk-wise execution, CUDA-stream overlap, visual token control, bounded visual attention, and query-side retrieval to bound per-chunk computation and memory costs. We further provide a systematic study of bottleneck migration, revealing how chunk size, token retention, attention locality, and retrieval scope shape the throughput-accuracy trade-off. Surgical world models address this by generating realistic, action-conditioned future frames from an initial observation, but existing methods exhibit two persistent failure modes: spatial interaction incoherence, where visible instrument contact fails to induce spatially consistent tissue deformation, and temporal fidelity collapse, where prediction errors compound across autoregressive rollouts and progressively corrupt visual quality. We present SurgVista, a surgical world model that mitigates both failures through two training recipes. Deformation Consistency Regularization extracts scene-point trajectories from training videos and enforces cross-frame coherence through latent contrastive learning, strengthening physically consistent instrument-tissue dynamics. ### [30] [Gaussian Process Prior Variational Autoencoder for Endoscopic Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19908)

Effective restoration therefore requires methods that exploit temporal continuity rather than treating frames in isolation. We introduce a Gaussian Process Prior Variational Autoencoder (GPVAE) framework for endoscopic video restoration that replaces the standard factorized latent prior with a temporal Gaussian process prior, enabling interpolation of missing frames with uncertainty-aware reconstruction.

Finally, the GP posterior provides per-frame uncertainty estimates that reflect temporal support and offer a confidence signal for restored frames.

TL;DR: SpatialSV is a framework that enhances multimodal large language models (MLLMs) with robust 3D spatial awareness by using task-oriented visual supervision to lift 2D features into explicit 3D representations like depth maps, camera poses, and point clouds. This approach offers interpretability through transparent 3D reconstructions, enabling diagnosis of spatial knowledge quality. It outperforms existing methods in spatial intelligence enhancement and generalizes well in semi-supervised settings.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing methods for enhancing MLLMs' spatial intelligence either rely on external tools with high inference overhead or use latent feature distillation that lacks interpretability and fine-grained geometric constraints. There is a need for an internalized, interpretable, and efficient way to learn 3D spatial awareness.

Method: SpatialSV introduces task-oriented visual supervision to actively transform 2D visual features into explicit 3D representations (depth maps, camera poses, point clouds). This process provides a transparent view into the model’s spatial understanding through reconstructible 3D outputs.

Result: Experiments across multiple models and benchmarks show SpatialSV effectively improves spatial intelligence in MLLMs. It also demonstrates strong generalization in semi-supervised scenarios, indicating potential for scalable, interpretable learning from unlabeled visual data.

Conclusion: SpatialSV successfully internalizes 3D spatial awareness in MLLMs with inherent interpretability and efficiency, offering a promising path toward more intelligent and transparent interaction with the 3D world.

Abstract: Unlocking the spatial intelligence of multimodal large language model (MLLMs) is crucial for understanding and interacting with the 3D world. Prevailing approaches typically inject spatial priors via external tools, which impose significant inference overhead, or rely on latent feature distillation, which remains uninterpretable and lacks fine-grained geometric constraints. To address these issues, we propose SpatialSV, a framework designed to internalize robust 3D spatial awareness within MLLMs while simultaneously offering inherent interpretability. Deviating from passive feature imitation, SpatialSV employs task-oriented visual supervision, compelling the model to actively lift its 2D visual features into explicit 3D representations, including depth maps, camera poses, and point clouds. Crucially, this 2D-to-3D lifting process provides a transparent window into the model's representations: the resulting 3D reconstructions serve as an intuitive proxy for visualizing and diagnosing the quality of the model's intrinsic spatial knowledge. Extensive experiments across multiple models and benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of SpatialSV in enhancing and interpreting MLLMs' spatial intelligence. Furthermore, the framework exhibits strong generalization in semi-supervised settings, validating its potential to leverage unlabeled visual data for scalable, interpretable spatial representation learning.

### [32] [CARE: Competence-Aware Reward Shaping for Adaptive Reasoning Length in Video-MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19927)
*Chengwen Liu,Hao Peng,Jisheng Dang,Hong Peng,Bin Hu,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CARE提出了一种基于能力感知的奖励塑造框架，用于多模态视频推理中的自适应推理长度优化。该方法通过指数移动平均估计模型能力，并据此引导训练进入不同阶段，从早期鼓励探索的长推理转向后期追求效率的简洁推理。为避免冗余与任务复杂度混淆，CARE引入批次级统计归一化和后验放大器，强化对历史难题表现突出样本的奖励信号。该机制无缝集成于GRPO训练流程，无额外推理开销。实验表明，CARE在多个视频理解基准上提升准确率、稳定RL训练并显著提高令牌效率，且推理长度呈现倒U型变化趋势，收敛时生成更短但信息量更高的推理轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于强化学习的多模态视频推理方法通常采用固定、僵化的推理长度控制策略，无法随模型能力动态调整，导致早期探索不足、后期冗余推理，影响训练效率与推理质量。

Method: CARE通过指数移动平均维护平滑的能力估计（pass rate），根据能力水平将训练分为渐进阶段，逐步改变奖励偏好：从鼓励长推理以促进探索，转向鼓励简洁推理以提升效率。同时引入批级统计归一化以分离冗余与真实复杂度，并设计后验放大器增强对困难样本中异常优异表现的奖励信号。整个机制嵌入GRPO训练流程，不增加推理开销。

Result: CARE在多个视频推理与通用视频理解数据集上均取得显著性能提升，不仅提高了推理准确率，还增强了强化学习的稳定性，大幅改善了令牌使用效率。训练过程中推理长度呈倒U型变化，最终收敛到更短但更具信息量的推理路径，验证了推理预算的合理分配。

Conclusion: CARE成功实现了多模态视频推理中推理长度的自适应优化，通过能力感知的奖励调节机制，有效平衡探索与效率，为高效、稳定的强化学习推理提供了新范式。代码已开源。

Abstract: In multimodal video reasoning, reinforcement learning-based methods typically rely on simplistic and inflexible reasoning-length control strategies that fail to adapt to the model's evolving competence. This mismatch may suppress necessary exploration at early stages, while encouraging redundant reasoning and inefficient decoding once the model becomes more competent. In this paper, we propose CARE, a competence-aware reward shaping framework for adaptive reasoning length optimization in multimodal reasoning. Specifically, CARE maintains a smoothed competence estimate via an exponential moving average of pass rates, and uses it to route training into progressive stages that shift the reward preference from exploration-oriented long-form reasoning to efficiency-oriented concise reasoning. To avoid conflating verbosity with intrinsic task complexity, CARE further normalizes reasoning effort with batch-level statistics, and introduces a posterior amplifier to strengthen reward signals for unexpectedly strong performance on historically difficult samples. The proposed mechanism is seamlessly integrated into the GRPO training pipeline and incurs no additional inference-time overhead. Extensive experiments on multiple video reasoning and general video understanding benchmarks demonstrate that CARE consistently improves reasoning accuracy, stabilizes reinforcement learning, and significantly enhances token efficiency. Moreover, CARE exhibits a characteristic inverted-U trajectory of reasoning length during training, and yields shorter yet more informative reasoning traces at convergence, indicating effective adaptive allocation of reasoning budget. We provide the source code for our proposed CARE framework and experiments at https://github.com/1Pansy/Video-CARE.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有光学流方法受限于特定网络架构、监督方式或数据集，缺乏普适性约束。为提升模型泛化能力与鲁棒性，需要一种不依赖具体模型假设、适用于多种场景的通用约束机制。

Method: 提出三角一致性约束，通过组合两组光学流（如图像对间的循环流、多帧间的时序链式流、或合成变换下的流）生成第三组流，并强制三者之间的一致性。该方法基于光学流的几何性质，无需额外标注，计算开销极低。

Abstract: We propose triangular consistency as a first-principled constraint for optical flow, which is agnostic to network architecture, supervision type, and dataset, and applies to both image-pair and multi-frame settings. This simple but powerful constraint is to compose two flows to induce a third flow and enforce consistency among the three. The composed flows may arise from (i) image pairs, yielding cycle consistency; (ii) multiple video frames, producing longer-range motion through temporal chaining; or (iii) image pairs combined with controlled synthetic transformations, which becomes data augmentation. This triangular consistency introduces negligible computational overhead and requires no additional annotations. Since it is derived directly from the geometry of optical flow, it does not rely on model-specific assumptions and serves as a ``universal'' plug-and-play component for optical flow training. Experiments show consistent improvement across supervised, unsupervised, and transfer learning settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖高成本的符号级边界框等空间监督，难以扩展；而手写数学表达式的二维布局和长程结构依赖使得生成极具挑战性。

Method: 设计了面向生成的Relational Abstract Syntax Tree (RelAST)，将MathML树压缩为紧凑的三元组序列[S, R, D]；引入MathVAE学习保持结构的潜在表示，通过符号感知和关系感知的正则化；采用MathDiT在结构化潜在空间中进行条件去噪，并通过自适应层归一化（AdaLN）引入全局符号计数先验以增强结构一致性。

Result: DiffMath生成的手写表达式具有更高的结构一致性，相比现有方法表现更优，并通过合成数据增强显著提升了下游OCR模型的准确率。

Conclusion: DiffMath成功实现了无需位置监督的高质量手写数学表达式生成，为大规模可扩展的数学表达式合成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Handwritten Mathematical Expression Generation (HMEG) is challenging due to the complex two-dimensional layouts and long-range structural dependencies of mathematical expressions. Existing methods typically rely on explicit spatial supervision, such as symbol-level bounding boxes, which incurs high annotation costs and limits scalability. In this work, we propose DiffMath, a symbol- and graph-aware latent diffusion framework that leverages the hierarchical structure inherent in LaTeX as a structural prior, eliminating the need for positional supervision. First, we design a Relational Abstract Syntax Tree (RelAST), a generation-oriented representation that distills MathML trees into compact triplet sequences [S, R, D], where each token directly encodes a symbol identity, spatial relation, or nesting depth. Second, we introduce MathVAE, which learns structure-preserving latent representations through symbol-aware and relation-aware perceptual regularization, ensuring that the latent space captures both character semantics and spatial topology. Third, MathDiT performs conditional denoising in this structured latent space, further guided by a global symbol-count prior via Adaptive Layer Normalization (AdaLN) to improve structural coherence. Experiments show that DiffMath produces structurally consistent handwritten expressions, achieves superior performance over existing methods, and improves the accuracy of downstream OCR models through synthetic data augmentation.

### [37] [Timage: A Generative Text-in-Image Paradigm for Fine-Tuning Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19944)
*Yifeng Wu,Huimin Huang,Ruiluo Wu,Chunyi Lin,Guanhua Chen,Xian Wu,Wang Song,Ruize Han*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入Timage，利用约束薛定谔桥（cSB）生成查询文本的图像叠加层。第一阶段为区域搜索，将噪声向与查询对齐的图像区域迁移，同时受硬遮挡屏障保护显著前景；第二阶段为外观塑造，通过‘墨水预算’正则化控制字符尺寸，确保文字清晰且视觉均衡。

Result: 在VMCBench基准测试中，Timage搭配7B规模的骨干模型显著优于更大的专有系统及参数调优基线，证明了其高效性和优越性能。

Conclusion: 该研究强调在输入层面进行有意的重建是一种强大且与架构无关的方法，能有效增强多模态推理中的空间语义对齐能力。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) often lose track of the right image regions during fine-grained spatial reasoning, because a textual query rarely carries any explicit geometric anchor into the pixel domain. Prevailing remedies either rewire the model's weights or pad the prompt with verbose instructions, yet neither reliably pins the language to the correct visual coordinates without eroding the backbone's general competence. We introduce Timage, a paradigm that recasts multimodal understanding as an alignment problem solved at the input: the query is drawn, as a typeset overlay, onto the image itself. The placement and appearance of this overlay are produced by a Constrained Schrödinger Bridge (cSB), an entropic optimal-transport sampler that factorizes layout synthesis into two coupled stochastic stages. The first stage, Region Search, transports noise toward query-aligned image zones while obeying a hard occlusion barrier that protects salient foreground content; the second stage, Appearance Shaping, sizes the glyphs through an ``ink-budget'' regularizer so that the rendered text stays legible and visually balanced. The resulting overlay behaves as an explicit attention beacon that channels the model's focus along spatial semantics. On the VMCBench suite, Timage paired with a modest 7B backbone clearly overtakes far larger proprietary systems as well as parameter-tuned baselines. The study positions deliberate input reconstruction as a powerful, architecture-neutral lever for strengthening multimodal reasoning.

*Meixi Li,Xianlin Zhang,Yue Zhang,Xueming Li*

TL;DR: SketchKeyAnime 是一种基于稀疏关键草图输入的视频扩散框架，能够生成结构可控、外观一致且时间连贯的动画。它通过双分支条件机制编码局部几何约束与语义-时间上下文，利用草图交叉注意力融合参考图像和草图条件，并采用自适应加权损失强化对关键草图帧和线稿区域的监督。在 Sakuga-42M 数据集的美学子集上，该方法显著优于现有基线，EDMD 降低 31.9%，FVD 降低 9.5%，在多数量化指标上表现最佳，验证了其在低成本、高可控动画生成中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动画制作依赖大量手工绘制和迭代优化，而现有动画生成方法通常需要完整的RGB边界帧、密集帧级条件或完整草图序列，难以适应低成本输入场景。因此，亟需一种能够在稀疏关键草图输入下实现高质量动画生成的方法。

Method: 提出 SketchKeyAnime 框架，采用双分支条件机制分别处理几何约束与语义-时间上下文；引入草图交叉注意力以融合参考图像与草图信息，并设计可学习门控机制；使用自适应加权损失强化关键帧和线稿区域的监督。

Result: 在 Sakuga-42M 美学子集上，相比最佳基线，SketchKeyAnime 在 EDMD 上减少 31.9%，在 FVD 上减少 9.5%，在多数定量指标上表现最优，证明其在草图保真度与时间连贯性方面具有显著优势。

Conclusion: SketchKeyAnime 成功实现了从稀疏关键草图输入生成高质量动画的目标，具备结构可控性、外观一致性与时间连贯性，为低资源、高可控动画创作提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Traditional animation production relies heavily on manual drawing and iterative refinement, particularly for key-pose design, in-betweening, and character coloring. While existing animation and video generation methods have made notable progress, they typically depend on RGB boundary frames, dense frame-wise conditions, or complete sketch sequences, limiting their applicability under low-cost input conditions. We present SketchKeyAnime, a video diffusion framework for generating structurally controllable, appearance-consistent, and temporally coherent animations from sparse key-sketch inputs. Given a single reference RGB image and a few temporally indexed key sketches, SketchKeyAnime introduces a dual-branch conditioning mechanism to encode local geometric constraints alongside semantic-temporal context. It leverages Sketch Cross Attention to fuse reference image and sketch conditions with learnable gating, and incorporates an Adaptive Weighted Loss to strengthen supervision on key-sketch frames and line-art regions. Experimental results on the Aesthetic subset of Sakuga-42M show that our approach consistently outperforms representative animation interpolation and sketch-guided generation baselines. Compared to the best-performing baseline, SketchKeyAnime reduces EDMD by 31.9\% and FVD by 9.5\%, demonstrating superior sketch fidelity and temporal coherence, while achieving the best overall performance across most quantitative metrics. These results validate the proposed framework and highlight its potential for low-cost, highly controllable animation creation.

### [40] [Addressing Detail Bottlenecks in Latent Diffusion for RGB-to-SWIR Image Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19961)
*Kaili Wang,Martin Dimitrievski,Jose Maria Salvador,Ben Stoffelen,David Van Hamme,Lore Goetschalckx*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出轻量级、与骨干网络无关的改进方法，解决潜在扩散模型在图像到图像翻译中丢失空间细节的问题。通过引入源条件自编码器（SCAE）和可学习引导编码器（LGE），显著提升检测性能，尤其在小物体上实现最高3.4倍的增益，并在多个基准上达到最优FID分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜在扩散模型在压缩过程中丢失精细空间信息，导致下游感知任务性能下降；主要瓶颈在于自编码器的信息损失和条件路径中的简单下采样操作。

Method: 设计Source-Conditioned Autoencoder (SCAE)，通过跳接将高分辨率源特征注入解码器；引入Learnable Guidance Encoder (LGE)，以可学习信号替代传统下采样，增强条件信息保留。

Result: 在RGB到SWIR图像转换任务中，检测mAP提升达2倍，小物体检测性能提升高达3.4倍（COCO-small），同时实现最先进的FID得分；验证了FID与检测性能之间的弱相关性，强调多维度评估的重要性。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效缓解了潜在扩散模型中的空间信息丢失问题，具有良好的泛化能力，适用于多种场景和骨干网络，为未来研究提供了新评估范式。

Abstract: Latent diffusion models (LDMs) enable efficient image-to-image translation but discard fine spatial details during compression, degrading downstream perception tasks. We identify two bottlenecks: the autoencoder, which loses spatial information, and the conditioning pathway, which further degrades the source signal through naive downsampling. We propose two lightweight, backbone-agnostic fixes: a Source-Conditioned Autoencoder (SCAE) that injects high-resolution source features into the decoder via skip connections, and a Learnable Guidance Encoder (LGE) that replaces naive downsampling with a learned conditioning signal. Evaluated on RGB-to-SWIR translation for driving scenes with two denoiser backbones (U-Net and DiT), our approach improves detection mAP by up to 2x over the latent diffusion baseline, with up to 3.4x gains on small objects (COCO-small, <32^2 px^2), while achieving state-of-the-art FID. We further show that FID and detection performance are poorly correlated, motivating multi-axis evaluation. Results generalise zero-shot to the public RASMD benchmark. We will publicly release test data with annotations, all checkpoints, and training code.

### [41] [ROSE: Benchmarking the Perception-to-Action Gap in Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19965)
*Yihao Wang,Zijian He,Jie Ren,Keze Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个名为ROSE的受控基准测试，用于评估多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在固定视觉场景下根据不同任务上下文执行相应动作的能力。通过耦合计数与坐标操作任务，检验模型是否能推断隐含的多数参考并基于细粒度视觉证据进行上下文相关的行动。结果显示，尽管人类表现高达98.8%，但九个主流MLLM在从计数任务转向区域条件动作任务时性能下降最高达44.5个百分点，且即使在模型正确计数的情况下仍存在显著差距。全局点击和局部匹配控制实验表明，坐标定位仅解释部分性能损失，揭示了模型在将共享视觉证据转化为特定上下文动作方面存在独立于定位的、模型依赖性的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型需要根据不同的任务上下文对同一视觉场景做出不同的行为响应，但现有模型在从视觉信息到上下文相关动作的转换中表现出显著能力不足，亟需一个可控的基准来系统评估其上下文敏感性与推理能力。

Method: 提出ROSE基准，固定视觉场景，通过改变区域约束和符号输出要求，设计耦合计数与坐标动作任务，以测试模型在不同上下文中对隐含多数参考的推断能力及细粒度视觉证据的利用能力。采用成对场景与区域进行对比分析，并引入全局点击和匹配局部控制作为对照实验，分离出坐标定位与上下文动作转换的影响。

Result: 九个主流多模态大语言模型在从计数任务过渡到区域条件动作任务时，性能下降最高达44.5个百分点；人类在相同任务上保持98.8%的准确率；即使模型在相同场景下正确计数，性能下降依然显著；控制实验表明坐标定位仅解释部分性能损失，表明存在独立于定位的、模型依赖性的瓶颈。

Conclusion: 当前多模态大语言模型在将共享视觉证据转化为上下文特定动作方面存在显著缺陷，其核心挑战并非视觉定位，而是如何根据任务上下文动态解析和响应视觉信息，这揭示了模型在语义理解与上下文推理方面的深层局限。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly expected to act on visual information, yet the same scene may require different actions under different task contexts. How reliably can a model turn the same visual evidence into the action required by the current context? To answer this question, we introduce \textsc{ROSE} (\textbf{R}eference-conditioned \textbf{O}ddity and \textbf{S}ymbolic \textbf{E}xecution), a controlled benchmark that holds the visual scene fixed while varying region constraints and required symbolic outputs. Through coupled counting and coordinate-action tasks, \textsc{ROSE} tests whether models can infer an implicit majority reference and act on the resulting fine-grained visual evidence under changing contexts. Across nine recent MLLMs, performance drops by as much as 44.5 percentage points from counting-oriented tasks to region-conditioned action, despite 98.8\% human performance. The gap persists on paired scenes and regions for which the same model returns the correct count, while global-click and matched local controls show that coordinate grounding explains only part of the loss, revealing a distinct, model-dependent bottleneck in turning shared visual evidence into context-specific actions.

### [42] [Semantic-Anchored Evidential Fusion for Domain-Robust Whole-Slide Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19966)
*Yucheng Xing,Ling Huang,Pei Liu,Jingying Ma,Jiaqing Xu,Kai He,Mengling Feng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为语义锚定证据融合生存分析（SAEFS）的新框架，旨在解决全切片图像（WSI）在跨临床中心应用中的泛化问题。该方法通过视觉问答（VQA）提取病理学语义锚点，结合双流视觉证据提取与基于狄利克雷的主观逻辑建模不确定性，利用谨慎合取规则融合语义与视觉证据，避免相关来源带来的过度自信融合。在仅在一个源域上训练、零样本跨四个未知域评估的情况下，SAEFS显著优于现有最先进模型，在预测准确性和可靠性方面均表现优异，平均C指数提升10.2%。定量分析显示，由VQA生成的语义特征在不同中心间的差异显著低于像素级特征，证明其具备更强的跨中心鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有WSI分析方法多关注域内性能，难以跨临床中心泛化，主要因依赖对染色和扫描仪硬件敏感的像素级表示。人类病理学家的诊断逻辑依赖于高阶病理语义（如肿瘤分级、微环境结构），这些语义具有领域不变性，可作为更稳健的表征基础。因此，亟需一种能捕捉此类语义信息并实现可靠跨域推理的方法。

Method: 提出SAEFS框架：1）使用视觉问答（VQA）从WSI中提取高阶病理语义锚点；2）采用双流架构分别提取视觉证据与语义证据；3）引入基于狄利克雷分布的主观逻辑模型来量化不确定性；4）通过谨慎合取规则融合语义与视觉证据，防止因相关性导致的过自信融合。

Result: 在零样本跨域测试中，SAEFS在四个未见中心上持续优于当前最优模型，平均C指数提升10.2%，表现出更高的预测准确性与可靠性。量化结果显示，VQA生成的语义特征在不同中心间差异显著小于像素特征，验证了其强鲁棒性与跨域适用性。

Conclusion: 高阶病理语义（如肿瘤分级、微环境结构）是跨临床中心泛化的理想表征，能够有效克服染色与设备差异带来的干扰。SAEFS框架通过语义锚定与不确定性的合理建模，实现了高性能且可靠的生存预测，为真实世界临床部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Whole-slide images (WSIs) are widely used for computational cancer prognosis. However, most existing methods primarily focus on in-domain performance and fail to generalize across clinical centers. This limitation stems from their reliance on pixel-derived representations that are highly susceptible to domain-specific artifacts caused by staining protocols and scanner hardware. We hypothesize that high-level pathology semantics, such as tumor grade and micro-environmental architecture, provide a domain-invariant semantic representation that mirrors the robust diagnostic logic of human pathologists. Therefore, we propose a Semantic-Anchored Evidential Fusion Survival (SAEFS) framework, where SAEFS derives semantic anchors from WSIs via Visual Question Answering (VQA), employs a dual-stream WSI evidence extraction architecture, uses Dirichlet-based Subjective Logic to model uncertainty, and fuses semantic and visual evidence through a cautious conjunction rule to avoid overconfident fusion from correlated sources. Trained exclusively on one source domain and evaluated zero-shot across four unseen domains, SAEFS consistently outperforms state-of-the-art models both in prediction accuracy and reliability, improving the average C-index by 10.2%. Quantitative analyses further show that VQA-derived semantic features exhibit significantly lower cross-center divergence than pixel-derived features, highlighting their robustness for cross-center clinical applications.

### [43] [CrossFlow: One-Step Generation Across Latent and Pixel Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19970)
*Xiyuan Wang,Xiao Zhang,Yang Li,Ruoxi Jiang,Zhao Zhong,Liefeng Bo,Muhan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CrossFlow提出一种跨空间流模型，将噪声潜变量直接映射到像素空间图像，通过无速度的一步目标实现潜空间轨迹与像素空间监督的结合，无需独立解码器，提升生成效率与质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散和流匹配生成器在统一表示空间中定义先验、概率路径和预测目标，虽然潜变量扩散提升了效率，但最终样本依赖于单独训练的解码器，导致生成潜变量与干净编码输出之间的不匹配，影响生成质量。

Method: 提出交叉空间流（CrossFlow），采用无速度的一步目标：潜变量轨迹用于训练路径，但监督预测为图像而非潜变量位移；模型可同时作为一步潜变量到像素生成器及潜变量扩散流水线中的解码器替代品。

Result: 在256×256的类条件ImageNet-1k上，CrossFlow-XL仅需一次函数评估即达到1.62 FID；消融实验表明潜变量编码器及像素空间感知和对抗损失对保真度至关重要。

Conclusion: 跨空间流目标能够结合潜变量表示的高效性与直接像素空间监督的优势，无需在推理时使用独立解码器，显著提升生成性能与效率。

Abstract: Most diffusion and flow-matching generators define the prior, probability path, and prediction target in the same representation space. Latent diffusion improves efficiency by moving this path into an autoencoder latent space, but the final sample is still produced by a separately trained decoder. This separation creates a mismatch: the generator is optimized for latent-space prediction, while final quality depends on how the decoder handles generated latents that may differ from clean encoder outputs. We introduce CrossFlow, a cross-space flow formulation that maps noisy latent inputs directly to pixel-space images. The key technical step is a velocity-free one-step objective: the latent trajectory defines the training path, but the supervised prediction is an image rather than a latent displacement. This lets one model act both as a one-step latent-to-pixel generator and as a decoder replacement for latent diffusion pipelines. On class-conditional ImageNet-1k at $256\times256$, CrossFlow-XL achieves 1.62 FID with one function evaluation. Ablations show that the latent encoder and pixel-space perceptual and adversarial losses are important for fidelity. These results indicate that cross-space flow objectives can combine the efficiency of latent representations with direct pixel-space supervision, without requiring a separate decoder at inference.

### [44] [Vision-Reasoning-Guided Occlusion Removal from Light Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19985)

Method: 首先利用光场积分（LFI）对多视角观测进行融合，以抑制前景遮挡并生成初步的增强可见性表示；随后引入视觉语言模型（VLM）作为条件语义先验，基于观测数据恢复退化的结构与细节；最后采用多样本融合策略，聚合多个生成假设以提高恢复一致性并减少幻觉伪影。

Abstract: Occlusion-robust scene recovery remains a major challenge in computational imaging, particularly in natural environments where dense foreground vegetation severely limits visibility. We propose a vision-reasoning-guided light field occlusion removal framework that combines the visibility recovery capability of light field integration (LFI) with the semantic reasoning capacity of vision-language models (VLMs). Multi-view observations are first integrated via LFI to suppress foreground occlusions and produce an initial visibility-enhanced representation. A VLM is then incorporated as a conditional semantic prior to restore degraded structures and recover fine details, guided by the observed measurements. To improve recovery consistency and reduce hallucination artifacts, we introduce a multi-sample fusion strategy that aggregates multiple generated hypotheses into a unified estimate. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving the highest average SSIM across four synthetic light field benchmark scenes (4-Syn) and strong generalization across structured and unstructured acquisition settings. We evaluate QG-MIL across six benchmarks spanning whole-slide pathology and cell-level hematology, covering two fundamentally different MIL scales. The best-performing QG-MIL variants outperform leading baselines on all six benchmarks, with an average improvement of +6.1 mean macro F1 points. Attention overlays and attention mass analysis confirm more distributed instance weighting. Ablation studies show that while individual components can match the full model on specific datasets, the QG-MIL design provides the most consistent cross-domain performance and tightest variance when compared to selected baselines.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放词汇变化检测方法在实例级比较中忽略细粒度语义变化，在像素级直接比较中因语义模糊性和空间不一致性导致结果不稳定和边界伪影，亟需一种兼顾灵活性与可靠性的新方法。

Method: 首先基于像素级语义差异生成候选变化区域；随后引入协同精炼策略，设计语义变化推理（SCR）模块，联合分析分布偏移与响应变异以抑制偶然不一致；并构建边界感知变化精炼（BCR）模块，通过内部像素可靠性验证来减少边界误判。

Result: 在LEVIR-CD、WHU-CD、DSIFN和SECOND等多个数据集上均取得显著性能提升，F₁^C指标提高2.13%至9.75%，同时具有更高的计算效率。

Conclusion: 所提ReA-OVCD框架有效解决了开放词汇变化检测中的可靠性问题，实现了灵活、精确且高效的细粒度变化识别，为未来遥感变化检测提供了新思路。

Abstract: Unlike traditional remote sensing change detection that relies on predefined categories, Open-Vocabulary Change Detection (OVCD) identifies land cover changes flexibly using arbitrary text prompts. However, existing methods suffer from an inherent trade-off when modeling changes: instance-level comparison overlooks fine-grained semantic variations (e.g., partial building extensions), while direct pixel comparison proves unreliable, yielding unstable responses and boundary artifacts due to semantic ambiguity and spatial inconsistency. To this end, we propose an efficient training-free Reliability-Aware Open-Vocabulary Change Detection (ReA-OVCD) framework. It first derives candidate change regions from pixel-wise semantic discrepancies to ensure flexible and detailed localization. To ensure reliability, it subsequently introduces a collaborative refinement strategy to explicitly model change validity from both semantic and spatial perspectives. Specifically, we develop a Semantic Change Reasoning (SCR) module that reassesses changes by jointly analyzing distributional divergence and response variation, enabling the suppression of incidental inconsistencies while preserving reliable semantic shifts. In addition, a Boundary-aware Change Refinement (BCR) module is designed to mitigate artifacts stemming from boundary misalignment and uncertainty through validating whether candidate regions are supported by reliable interior pixels. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets (LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, DSIFN, and SECOND) demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms state-of-the-art approaches, achieving $\mathrm{F}_{1}^{C}$ improvements of 2.13\% to 9.75\% with higher computational efficiency. The code is publicly available at \https://github.com/Funny0101/ReA-OVCD

### [47] [PU-UNet: Stable Multiplicative Interactions for Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20035)

TL;DR: 提出PU-UNet，一种基于稳定乘积单元的残差U-Net，用于医学图像分割。通过平滑正映射与对数域截断结合，实现稳定的乘法特征学习，计算开销极小。在ISIC 2018、Kvasir-SEG和BUSI数据集上表现优异，显著提升Dice和IoU，同时保持参数量、计算量和推理延迟几乎不变，并大幅降低正常样本的假阳性率。消融实验表明乘积单元交互是关键，且在低分辨率阶段效果最佳，稳定性设计至关重要。

Abstract: Many dense prediction networks rely on additive feature transformations and model higher-order feature interactions only implicitly. Product units provide an explicit mechanism for multiplicative feature modeling, but their logarithmic--exponential formulation can cause numerical instability, which has limited their use in deep dense prediction networks. In this work, we propose Product-Unit U-Net (PU-UNet), a residual U-Net that integrates stable product-unit residual blocks into rich low-resolution stages for medical image segmentation. Compared with a matched Residual U-Net baseline, PU-UNet consistently improves Dice and IoU while keeping parameters, FLOPs, and inference latency nearly unchanged, and reduces the image-level false-positive rate on normal BUSI cases from 0.077 to zero. Ablation studies suggest that the gains are associated with product-unit interactions, are strongest under low-resolution placement, and benefit from the proposed stabilization design. These results suggest that stable product-unit residual learning can be an effective way to enhance U-Net-style segmentation networks with explicit multiplicative interactions.

Abstract: Despite significant progress in multi-modal Re-Identification (ReID), existing methods tend to emphasize low-frequency cues. Consequently, they focus on attributes such as color, illumination, and coarse appearance, while overlooking mid and high-frequency structures that encode geometric, textural, and identity-discriminative details. This imbalance leads to incomplete spectral representations and unstable cross-modal alignment.
