Method: FlexLAM采用嵌套丢弃训练可变长度的潜在动作，生成前缀有效的编码，使模型先捕捉紧凑的过渡结构，再按需添加细节，无需修改网络结构或引入额外损失函数。

Result: 单一FlexLAM在各种令牌预算下均达到或超过独立训练的固定容量LAMs的表现，尤其在稀疏标签监督和低回报单任务对齐压力测试中优势明显；支持推理时动态调整令牌预算，且显著提升Ego4D过渡重建性能。

Conclusion: 可变长度潜在动作是一种无需架构变更、可直接替换现有固定容量瓶颈的升级方案，适用于潜在动作模型、潜在动作世界模型及视频预训练动作接口。

Abstract: Latent actions provide a compact interface between action-free video and downstream decision-making, yet existing Latent Action Models (LAMs) force every transition through a fixed-capacity bottleneck. We identify a bottleneck trade-off: overly tight codes can discard transition cues needed for action alignment, while overly loose codes preserve additional transition variation that must be resolved when alignment labels are scarce or narrowly distributed. FlexLAM replaces this fixed capacity with variable-length latent actions trained by nested dropout, yielding prefix-valid codes that capture compact transition structure first and add detail only when needed, without new architectures or losses. A single FlexLAM matches or surpasses separately trained fixed-capacity LAMs at every evaluated token budget under standard scarce-label supervision and under a low-return single-task alignment stress test, indicating that FlexLAM is not merely adjustable at inference time but learns a better latent-action interface at the same token budgets. The same model supports inference-time token-budget adjustment without retraining, and FlexLAM improves Ego4D transition reconstruction. These results suggest that variable-length latent actions are an architecture-free, drop-in upgrade to the fixed-capacity bottleneck in latent action models, latent-action world models, and video-pretrained action interfaces.

### [177] [Spectral DPPs via NEPv: A Scalable Continuous Relaxation of Determinantal MAP for Diversity-Aware Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19411)
*Richard Yi Da Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将确定性点过程（DPP）的MAP目标重新表述为在Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题，揭示其一阶最优性条件构成一种新型非线性特征值问题（NEPv），并提出基于自洽场（SCF）迭代的求解方法。该方法具有基于谱间隙的局部收敛保证，计算复杂度近线性于候选集大小n，仅需矩阵-向量乘法，适用于大规模机器学习场景中的多样子集选择任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模机器学习中，从海量候选数据中选取小而多样、高质量的子集是一个常见挑战，如数据筛选、核心集选择、主动学习、提示选择等。虽然确定性点过程（DPP）提供了良好的多样性建模方式，但其最大后验（MAP）目标是NP难的，传统贪婪和采样算法随候选集规模超线性增长，难以应用于实际的大规模场景。

Method: 将DPP-MAP问题转化为Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题，推导出其对应的非线性特征值问题（NEPv），设计基于自洽场（SCF）的迭代求解算法。该方法利用特征向量依赖的算子，通过矩阵-向量乘法实现高效计算，并具备基于谱间隙的局部收敛性保证。

Result: 提出的算法\OurMethod在每次迭代中仅需$O(ndk + nk^2)$时间，总时间为$O((ndk+nk^2)t)$，其中$t$为迭代次数，实现了近线性于候选集大小$n$的可扩展性。该方法可直接与低秩核和特征映射核结合，适用于现代机器学习中的大规模多样性选择任务。

Conclusion: 本工作为大规模多样性子集选择提供了一个理论严谨且高效可扩展的求解框架，通过连续松弛与自洽场迭代，突破了传统DPP方法在规模上的瓶颈，为未来实证研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Selecting a small, diverse, high-quality subset from a massive pool of candidates is a recurring primitive in modern machine learning -- data curation and coreset selection for training and fine-tuning large models, active-learning batch acquisition, prompt and exemplar selection for in-context learning, retrieval diversification, and experimental design. Determinantal Point Processes (\DPP s) give a principled, well-calibrated notion of diversity for this task, but their \emph{MAP} objective -- pick a size-$k$ subset $S$ maximizing $\logdet(L_S)$ -- is NP-hard, and the standard greedy and sampling algorithms scale superlinearly in the ground-set size $n$. This cost is prohibitive precisely in the data-centric regime where diversity matters most, where $n$ ranges over millions to billions of candidate examples, features, or embeddings. We recast \DPP-MAP as a continuous optimization problem over the Stiefel manifold, and show that its first-order optimality conditions form a \emph{Nonlinear Eigenvalue Problem with eigenvector dependency} (\NEPv) of a previously unstudied form. This \NEPv\ admits a self-consistent field (\SCF) iteration with a spectral-gap-based local contraction guarantee, giving a principled iterative solver where the diversity objective drives an eigenvector-dependent operator. The resulting algorithm, \OurMethod, requires only matrix-vector products with the kernel and runs in time $O\!\big((ndk+nk^2)\,t\big)$ for a small number of iterations $t$, scaling near-linearly in $n$ and integrating directly with low-rank and feature-map kernels common in ML. This paper focuses on the relaxation, solver, and scaling analysis; full real-data benchmarking is left to a planned empirical study.

Abstract: Time series forecasting leverages historical patterns to predict future values, but traditional methods face challenges when dealing with complex, non-stationary patterns that are difficult to memorize during training. Retrieval-augmented approaches have emerged as promising solutions by retrieving similar historical patterns to enhance predictions. However, existing retrieval methods suffer from two fundamental limitations: spectral blindness, which overlooks critical frequency-domain characteristics that capture underlying periodic structures, and temporal recency, which treats all historical data equally without emphasizing recent, more relevant patterns. In this paper, we propose SpecReTF, a novel retrieval method that addresses these issues by converting time series into windowed frequency representations, measuring similarity with a combined metric that captures both amplitude and phase information. To balance recency and historical context, we apply an exponential moving average weighting scheme that emphasizes recent windows. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets demonstrate that SpecReTF outperforms time-domain retrieval methods, achieving superior forecasting accuracy across diverse, non-stationary time series.

### [179] [Does Text Actually Help? Uncovering and Resolving Text Collapse in Multimodal Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19413)
*Huu Hiep Nguyen,Minh Hoang Nguyen,Dung Nguyen,Hung Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出REST-TS，一种针对多模态时间序列预测中“文本坍缩”问题的新方法。通过将数值分支与文本分支的不对称性转化为设计原则，让数值分支独立生成预测，而文本分支则专门监督残差部分（即数值无法解释的预测差距），从而迫使文本分支真正提取输入描述中的有效信息。实验表明，REST-TS在多个真实场景和架构下均达到最优性能，并显著提升文本分支的利用率，验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架在多模态时间序列预测中存在‘文本坍缩’问题，即文本分支收敛为不依赖内容的变换，贡献极少判别信息。这源于数值输入与输出间的强自相关性使数值分支主导模型，而文本分支未被充分使用，导致其功能被系统性低估。

Method: 提出REST-TS方法，利用数值分支生成独立预测，文本分支仅被监督以预测数值无法解释的残差部分。由于数值路径无法减少残差损失，文本分支必须从输入描述中提取真实语义信息，从而避免坍缩。

Result: REST-TS在多种真实世界领域和骨干网络架构上均取得当前最佳性能，且文本分支的利用率显著高于现有方法，证明其能有效激发文本分支的真实内容提取能力。

Conclusion: 通过将时间序列预测中的数值-文本不对称性转化为设计优势，REST-TS成功缓解了文本坍缩问题，实现了更高效、更具解释性的多模态时间序列预测。

Abstract: Multimodal time series forecasting, which pairs numerical sequences with domain-relevant textual reports, promises to inject world knowledge into forecasting pipelines. However, we uncover a critical failure mode in existing frameworks that we term text collapse: the text branch converges to a content-independent transformation, contributing negligible discriminative signal regardless of the input description. We argue that text collapse is a consequence of a fundamental asymmetry in time series forecasting: the numerical input is strongly autocorrelated with the output, making the numerical backbone inherently dominant, while the text branch, despite carrying complementary and often critical information, is insufficiently utilized, leading to its systematic underexploitation. To address this, we propose \textbf{REST-TS} (\textbf{R}esidual-\textbf{E}xclusive \textbf{S}upervision for \textbf{T}ext in \textbf{T}ime \textbf{S}eries), which turns the asymmetry into a design principle: the numerical backbone produces its own independent numerical forecast, and the text branch is exclusively supervised to predict the structured components of the residual, the prediction gap that numbers cannot explain. Because no numerical pathway can reduce these losses, the text branch must extract genuine content from the input description. Evaluated across diverse real-world domains and backbone architectures, REST-TS achieves state-of-the-art performance and consistently demonstrates greater text-branch utilization than existing frameworks, providing strong empirical evidence that supervising the text branch on the residual compels it to extract genuine content from the input.

</details>


### [180] [MortarBench: Evaluating Mortgage Loan Origination Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19416)
*Matthew Toles,Yunan Lu,Manav Munjal,Bojun Liu,Yuanhao Deng,Stephanie Selig,Derek Rindner,Cheng Li,Zhou Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MortarBench，一个用于评估贷款发起代理的基准测试，通过金融数据合成与变异生成覆盖广泛边缘情况的真实世界分布样本。实验发现当前最先进的大语言模型（LLMs）表现不佳，闭源模型最高仅达到77.1%的精确匹配准确率，并存在对非英语姓名的系统性偏见。为此，作者提出CRIT框架，一种置信度校准方法，将准确率提升至80.5%，同时改善风险控制能力并降低偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前贷款发起过程中虽有企业引入贷款代理以辅助人类贷款官，但缺乏公开的评估基准。为填补这一空白，需要一个能够全面评估贷款代理性能的基准测试，以揭示现有大语言模型在实际应用中的局限性及其潜在偏见。

Method: 构建MortarBench基准测试，采用金融数据合成与变异管道生成具有广泛边缘案例覆盖且符合真实世界分布的数据样本；使用该基准评估现有大语言模型性能；识别模型在非英语姓名上的系统性偏见；设计并实现CRIT（信心校准）框架以改进模型表现和减少偏见。

Result: 大语言模型在MortarBench上表现有限，闭源模型最高准确率为77.1%；模型对非英语姓名存在系统性偏见；引入CRIT框架后，准确率提升至80.5%，风险控制能力增强，偏见显著降低。

Conclusion: MortarBench有效揭示了当前大语言模型在贷款发起任务中的不足与偏见。通过引入CRIT置信度校准框架，显著提升了模型准确性与公平性，为未来贷款代理系统的开发与评估提供了可靠工具与方向。

Abstract: Loan origination is the process by which a lender creates a new loan, from application and underwriting through approval and funding. This process serves a critical role in evaluating the eligibility and level of risk posed by an applicant. Recently, firms have begun using mortgage loan agents to augment human loan officers, despite a lack of any public benchmark. To fill this gap, we present MortarBench, a loan origination agent benchmark. MortarBench uses a financial data synthesis and mutation pipeline to generate examples with broad edge case coverage that match real-world distributions and questions. We find that state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs) perform poorly, with closed-source models achieving at most 77.1\% exact match accuracy. We also discover systematic biases in LLM perception of foreignness related to non-English names. Noting these weaknesses, we introduce CRIT, a confidence calibration framework. Our method increases accuracy to 80.5\% while improving risk management steering and reducing bias.

</details>


### [181] [3D-DLP: Self-Supervised 3D Object-Centric Scene Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19451)
*Ellina Zhang,Madhaven Iyengar,Amir Zadeh,Chuan Li,Deepak Pathak,David Held,Tal Daniel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 3D-DLP是一种自监督的、以物体为中心的表示学习模型，将场景级的RGB-D或体素观测分解为一组3D潜在粒子。每个粒子编码解耦属性（如3D关键点位置、边界框尺寸和外观特征），代表场景中的一个独立实体。通过端到端的自监督重建目标，模型学习可解释的逐粒子分割图。实验表明，该方法在模拟和真实数据集上均能生成可解释且可控的潜在空间，通过操纵粒子位置和解码可生成新场景配置。此外，利用这些紧凑的3D潜在粒子进行下游机器人操作任务，性能优于缺乏显式3D信息或依赖高内存密集型3D输入的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理3D场景时，要么缺乏显式的3D结构信息，要么依赖计算量大、内存密集的3D输入，难以实现可解释性和可控性。因此，需要一种能够从场景中提取具有解耦属性的物体级表示，并支持高效推理与操控的方法。

Method: 基于深度潜在粒子（DLP）框架，3D-DLP将场景分解为一组3D潜在粒子，每个粒子编码包括3D关键点位置、边界框维度和外观特征等解耦属性。通过端到端的自监督重建目标，学习可解释的逐粒子分割图，并实现对粒子的可操控性。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界数据集上验证了模型的可解释性和可控性：可通过调整粒子位置与解码生成新颖的场景配置；在下游机器人操作任务中表现优于基线方法，尤其在不依赖密集3D输入的前提下展现出更高效率与性能。

Conclusion: 3D-DLP成功实现了从场景中提取可解释、可操控的物体级3D表示，为机器人感知与操作提供了高效且结构清晰的解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce 3D-DLP, a self-supervised object-centric representation learning model that decomposes scene-level RGB-D or voxel observations into a set of 3D latent particles. Building on the Deep Latent Particles (DLP) framework, each particle encodes disentangled attributes, including 3D keypoint position, bounding box dimensions, and appearance features, and represents a distinct entity in the scene. The model learns interpretable per-particle segmentation maps through an end-to-end self-supervised reconstruction objective. We demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that the learned latent space is interpretable and controllable: by manipulating particle positions and decoding, we can generate novel scene configurations. Furthermore, we show that leveraging these compact 3D latent particles for downstream robotic manipulation improves performance over baselines that either lack explicit 3D information or rely on memory-intensive dense 3D inputs without object-centric structure. Code and videos are available at https://eubooks3003.github.io/3d-dlp.

</details>


### [182] [Can In-Context Learning Support Intrinsic Curiosity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19476)
*Eric Elmoznino,Sangnie Bhardwaj,Johannes von Oswald,Rajai Nasser,Blaise Agüera y Arcas,João Sacramento,Rif A. Saurous,Guillaume Lajoie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用序列模型的上下文学习能力来解决机器学习中的数据选择问题，提出了一种无需梯度更新的内在好奇心机制。虽然在一般马尔可夫决策过程中该方法存在偏差，但在非时序场景（如主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计）中，基于上下文学习的奖励能有效逼近真实的学习进度，并在实验中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统探索奖励依赖于梯度更新的内循环计算，成本过高，难以规模化。因此需要一种更高效的替代方案来实现自动数据选择。

Method: 利用序列模型的上下文学习能力作为即时、无需更新的世界模型，通过预测误差和反事实上下文扰动来构建内在奖励信号，评估其能否准确反映学习进度。

Result: 理论上证明，在一般马尔可夫决策过程中，该方法无法无偏估计学习进度；但在非时序设置下，该方法能有效边界化并渐近收敛到真实学习进度。实验表明，该框架能够训练出高效探索的数据收集策略。

Conclusion: 在非时序任务中，基于上下文学习的内在好奇心机制是可行且有效的，为大规模自动化数据选择提供了新路径，但在时序环境中仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: Effective machine learning depends not only on how we model data, but also on what data we choose to collect. While large sequence models have revolutionized data modeling, the problem of automated data selection, or "intrinsic curiosity", remains a significant challenge. Classic approaches incentivize exploration by rewarding an agent based on its "learning progress", which measures how much a newly acquired observation improves a world model's predictive ability. However, evaluating these rewards traditionally requires expensive inner loops of gradient descent updates within each trajectory, rendering them computationally impractical at scale. In this work, we investigate whether the emergent in-context learning (ICL) capabilities of sequence models can eliminate this bottleneck by serving as immediate, update-free world models. Specifically, we evaluate whether an exploration policy can be trained to maximize learning progress, using solely the prediction errors and counterfactual context manipulations of an in-context learner. We first prove that in general Markov decision processes, this is in fact impossible in an unbiased way: the resulting intrinsic rewards either suffer from nuisance terms that bias their estimation of true learning progress, or they cannot be implemented using an in-context learner's prediction errors. Conversely, we prove a positive result for a broad subclass of non-temporal settings, encompassing active learning and Bayesian Experimental Design: here, ICL-derived rewards successfully bound and asymptotically converge to the true learning progress. We corroborate our theory with controlled experiments across continuous and symbolic environments, demonstrating that our ICL-driven framework successfully trains curious data-collection policies that explore optimally.

Conclusion: Insulin4RL为医疗领域离线强化学习提供了高质量、真实世界的数据基础，有助于推动更可靠、更具临床实用性的智能决策系统发展，未来可探索动态策略优化、不确定性建模与多中心泛化等方向。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement learning (ORL) offers the potential to improve the quality of clinical decision-making using historical electronic health record (EHR) data. Current training and evaluative practices in this field rely heavily on EHR datasets that have been temporally discretised into fixed, regular time intervals. Discretisation creates fictional representations of complex clinical scenarios and compromises the generalisability of retrospective model evaluations. In this paper, we introduce Insulin4RL, a healthcare ORL dataset featuring naturally irregular inputs and actions from real clinical trajectories. Derived from MIMIC-IV, Insulin4RL comprises over 375,000 labelled decisions across 12,209 patients requiring insulin infusion titration in the Intensive Care Unit. The dataset can thus be used for research into ORL model performance under realistic clinical sampling assumptions. We provide a description of the dataset's structure and characteristics, baseline performance metrics using model-free offline reinforcement learning, and a standardised evaluation protocol using fitted Q-evaluation. We conclude with suggested areas for future research that could be addressed using this resource.

### [184] [Concept Flow Models: Anchoring Concept-Based Reasoning with Hierarchical Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19489)
*Ya Wang,Adrian Paschke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出概念流模型（CFMs），通过层次化决策树替代传统平面瓶颈结构，聚焦局部判别性概念，逐步缩小预测范围，有效减少信息泄露，提升可解释性与可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视觉-语言模型的解释性方法在概念数量接近嵌入维度时易产生信息泄露，导致模型利用无关相关性，削弱可解释性。

Method: 构建从视觉嵌入生成的层次化决策树，分层分配语义概念，并通过概率遍历训练可微概念权重。

Result: CFMs在多个基准上达到与平面CBMs相当的预测性能，显著降低有效概念使用量和信息泄露，实现透明、可审计的分步推理。

Conclusion: CFMs通过层次化概念决策机制，在保持高性能的同时，大幅提升了模型的可解释性和可信度。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) enhance interpretability by projecting learned features into a human-understandable concept space. Recent approaches leverage vision-language models to generate concept embeddings, reducing the need for manual concept annotations. However, these models suffer from a critical limitation: as the number of concepts approaches the embedding dimension, information leakage increases, enabling the model to exploit spurious or semantically irrelevant correlations and undermining interpretability. In this work, we propose Concept Flow Models (CFMs), which replace the flat bottleneck with a hierarchical, concept-driven decision tree. Each internal node in the hierarchy focuses on a localized subset of discriminative concepts, progressively narrowing the prediction scope. Our framework constructs decision hierarchies from visual embeddings, distributes semantic concepts at each hierarchy level, and trains differentiable concept weights through probabilistic tree traversal. Extensive experiments on diverse benchmarks demonstrate that CFMs match the predictive performance of flat CBMs, while substantially mitigating information leakage by reducing effective concept usage. Furthermore, CFMs yield stepwise decision flows that enable transparent and auditable model reasoning with hierarchical class structures.

</details>


### [185] [Algebraic Dead Directions in LayerNorm Transformers: A Forward-Pass-Only Diagnostic at LLM Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19491)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar,P. J. Narayanan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种仅通过LayerNorm缩放参数即可直接读取预训练Transformer中“死方向”（dead directions）的方法。该方向为LayerNorm仿射变换的逆尺度方向 $γ^{-1}/\|γ^{-1}\|$，在任意输入分布下精确对应于最终归一化后激活协方差的核空间，无需前向传播或特征分解。实验验证了其在14个预训练模型（9个LayerNorm、5个RMSNorm，规模160M-35B）上的有效性：随机初始化时与实测最小奇异方向高度一致（四位小数精度），且在无均值减法投影的RMSNorm模型中缺失。训练后该方向的协方差特征值增强约1000倍，揭示了从随机初始化到训练状态的奇异结构演化。该方法可闭式推导出残差流最小奇异值的块间保持性，并实现仅凭参数判断归一化类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法检测死方向需依赖前向传播、激活特征分解或采样估计，无法仅从参数直接获取。本文旨在寻找一种仅由网络参数决定、计算成本极低的精确死方向读取方式，尤其针对广泛使用的LayerNorm结构。

Method: 提出并证明了LayerNorm的逆尺度方向 $γ^{-1}/\|γ^{-1}\|$ 是后最终归一化激活协方差的精确代数核，从而构成参数空间中的死方向。该方向可直接从层归一化缩放参数计算，无需任何前向或反向传播，也无需特征值分解。通过理论推导和大规模实验验证其在不同模型架构与训练状态下的有效性。

Result: 在9个LayerNorm模型中，随机初始化时预测方向与实测最小奇异方向匹配至四位小数；在5个RMSNorm模型中该方向缺失，符合预期。训练后该方向的协方差特征值显著增大（~10^3倍），揭示训练带来的奇异结构变化。此外，该方向可闭式推导出残差流最小奇异值的块间保持性，并能准确分类归一化类型。

Conclusion: 该研究首次提出一种仅依赖参数即可精确读取死方向的方法，适用于所有使用均值减法的归一化结构（如LayerNorm）。该方法具有极低计算开销，且可揭示模型从随机初始化到训练完成的奇异结构演化过程，具备理论与应用双重价值。

Abstract: Pretrained transformers sit near singular minima of the loss, where the Fisher information metric degenerates along dead directions: directions in parameter space along which the directional Fisher vanishes. Locating such a direction normally needs a forward pass and an eigendecomposition of activations, or a sampling-based complexity estimate; none returns a direction computable from the network's parameters alone. We give one, for LayerNorm transformers. The inverse-scale direction $γ^{-1}/\|γ^{-1}\|$ of the LayerNorm affine is an exact algebraic kernel of the post-final-norm centred activation covariance, for any input distribution, and induces a corresponding dead direction in parameter space. It is read from the LN scale parameter alone, with no forward or backward pass and no eigensolve: the cheapest dead-direction read, specific to LayerNorm. We test it on $14$ pretrained transformers ($9$ LayerNorm, $5$ RMSNorm; $160$M-$35$B; language and vision objectives). At random initialisation the predicted direction matches the measured bottom singular direction (one forward pass, direct SVD) to four decimal places on $9/9$ LayerNorm models, and is correctly absent on $5/5$ RMSNorm models, which lack the mean-subtraction projector that creates it. On the trained checkpoint the covariance eigenvalue along this direction deepens by ${\sim}10^3\times$ and further dead directions open; the random-init-to-trained gap is a one-forward-pass, per-checkpoint readout of singular structure along the predicted coordinate. Two consequences follow in closed form: the residual stream's smallest singular value is preserved block-to-block on $13/14$ transformers measured on their own input distribution, the one exception (Gemma$4$-$31$B) a genuine dead direction the same read pinpoints; and the kernel direction's presence classifies a transformer's normalisation from the parameters alone.

</details>


### [186] [Calibrating Generative Models to Feature Distributions with MMD Finetuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19496)
*Nathaniel L. Diamant,Brian L. Trippe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为kCGM的生成模型校准方法，通过最小化生成数据与目标数据在特征分布上的最大均值差异（MMD），同时结合KL正则化保持与预训练模型的接近性，有效解决生成样本在关键特征分布上偏离目标的问题。该方法在抗生素、蛋白质和DNA生成任务中均表现出色，能适配多种生成模型架构，并仅依赖特征级监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型在微调时容易过拟合，且无法精确控制哪些特征被匹配，导致生成结果虽在某些特征上接近目标分布，但整体化学或生物有效性下降。因此需要一种既能精准匹配特征分布又不牺牲生成质量的方法。

Method: 提出kernel Calibrating Generative Models (kCGM)，利用无偏得分函数估计器最小化生成数据与目标数据之间的最大均值差异（MMD），并引入KL散度正则化以保持与原始预训练模型的一致性，从而实现对特征分布的精准校准而不破坏生成样本的有效性。

Result: 在174种抗生素的目标集上，直接微调会牺牲化学有效性来匹配特征分布，而kCGM在提升特征匹配度的同时显著提高了生成分子的有效性；该方法还成功应用于蛋白质和DNA生成任务，适用于自回归、连续空间扩散及离散扩散模型，仅需特征级监督即可实现良好性能。

Conclusion: kCGM提供了一种高效且通用的生成模型校准框架，能够在不损失生成质量的前提下精准匹配目标特征分布，适用于多种生成任务和模型架构，为可控生成提供了新思路。

Abstract: Generative models can produce individually plausible samples while deviating substantially from a target set in the distribution of key features. For example, a model pretrained on broad drug-like chemical space may generate molecules whose molecular features differ from those of a therapeutic class of interest, such as known antibiotics. Correcting such distributional miscalibration is challenging: direct finetuning on the target set can overfit and does not control which features are matched. To fill this gap, we introduce kernel Calibrating Generative Models (kCGM). kCGM minimizes a maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between generated and target feature distributions using an unbiased score-function estimator, with KL regularization to remain close to the pretrained model. On a target set of 174 antibiotics, direct finetuning sacrifices chemical validity for feature-distribution matching, whereas kCGM improves target feature matching while increasing validity. We further demonstrate kCGM in protein and DNA generation tasks, showing it can adapt autoregressive, continuous-space diffusion, and discrete diffusion models using only feature-level supervision. Code is available at https://github.com/smithhenryd/cgm.

</details>


### [187] [Interactive Pareto navigation for deep multi-task learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19521)
*Augustina C. Amakor,Konstantin Sonntag,Sebastian Peitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为偏好帕累托探索（PPE）的新框架，用于多任务学习中在不显式计算海森矩阵的情况下，通过预测-校正方法在帕累托最优解流形上沿决策者偏好方向进行交互式探索，利用自动微分高效获取矩阵-向量乘积，提升效率与鲁棒性，并在模拟问题和深度学习实例中验证了其有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多任务学习中随着目标数量增加，传统加权求和损失的方法难以捕捉决策者的偏好或帕累托前沿的几何特性，且需大量调整与计算，成本高昂。

Method: 引入基于预测-校正方法的偏好帕累托探索（PPE）框架，预测步骤沿帕累托最优解流形的切线方向遵循决策者偏好，校正步骤生成反映该偏好的新权衡；采用克雷洛夫子空间方法避免显式海森矩阵计算，仅依赖自动微分获得矩阵-向量乘积。

Result: PPE在多个玩具问题和深度学习应用中表现出良好的功能性和性能，能够在不牺牲效率的前提下有效处理复杂多目标优化中的偏好与几何结构。

Conclusion: PPE提供了一种高效、稳健且可交互的多任务学习优化框架，能够准确反映决策者偏好并适应帕累托集的几何结构，适用于高维深度学习场景。

Abstract: In multi-task learning, handling an increasing number of objectives can quickly become challenging, both in terms of the computational resources and the decision maker's capacity to choose appropriate trade-offs. A widely used approach is thus to aggregate the individual losses in a single loss function by a weighted sum. This often fails to capture either the decision maker's preferences as a result of the shape of the Pareto front, or requires multiple adjustments and computations which becomes prohibitively expensive in deep learning applications. To address these issues, we introduce a novel framework, Preference Pareto Exploration (PPE), which enforces the decision maker's preferences while accounting for the geometry of the Pareto set in an interactive exploration process. PPE is based on a predictor-corrector method that performs predictor steps tangential to the manifold of Pareto-optimal solutions, following the decision maker's preference. The subsequent corrector step results in a new trade-off reflecting this preference. To avoid explicit Hessian computations when characterizing the tangent space of the manifold, we employ a Krylov subspace method that relies solely on matrix-vector products. These products can be efficiently obtained via automatic differentiation, ensuring both efficiency and robustness throughout the optimization process. The method's functionality and performance are demonstrated using both toy problems and examples from deep learning.

</details>


### [188] [Techniques for Peak Memory Reduction for LoRA Fine-tuning of LLMs on Edge Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19528)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在消费者硬件上使用LoRA对大语言模型进行微调虽能实现个性化且保护数据隐私，但面临严重的内存限制，尤其在处理数十亿参数和长上下文数据时，峰值内存常超出设备容量。

Method: 提出四种互补方法：(1) 基础模型量化配合实时反量化；(2) 结合选择性激活缓存与磁盘卸载的内存高效检查点；(3) 基于语义相关词元子集的softmax近似；(4) logits掩码。

Result: 在Llama-3.2 3B和Qwen-2.5 3B模型上，峰值内存分别降低26倍和28倍，实现了在资源受限设备上的高效微调，同时保持模型质量。

Conclusion: 所提出的多技术协同方案有效突破了消费级设备在大模型微调中的内存瓶颈，为端侧个性化模型训练提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Fine-tuning of Large Language Models (LLMs) using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) on an end-user's data offers personalized experiences while keeping data private, but faces severe memory constraints on consumer hardware. Peak memory during fine-tuning often exceeds device limits, especially for models with billions of parameters and long-context training data. This paper introduces a suite of complementary techniques to reduce memory footprint without sacrificing model quality: (1) base model quantization with on-the-fly dequantization, (2) memory-efficient checkpointing combining selective activation caching and disk offloading, (3) softmax approximation using semantically relevant token subsets, and (4) logits masking. Experiments on Llama-3.2 3B and Qwen-2.5 3B demonstrate up to $26\times$ and $28\times$ reduction in peak memory, enabling fine-tuning on resource-constrained devices.

Result: 多数拓扑重组发生在训练早期，出现瞬时拓扑活动峰值后快速稳定；不同对齐目标产生可区分的拓扑轨迹，指令微调与预训练模型具有显著不同的演化模式。

Abstract: Large language models are commonly aligned through supervised fine-tuning, yet little is known about how their internal representations evolve during this process. We study alignment dynamics using persistent homology by tracking the topology of activation spaces throughout fine-tuning. A dense checkpoint analysis reveals a transient peak in topological activity followed by rapid stabilization. ### [190] [Predicting Mergeability of Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19549)
*Lin Tang,Wei Zhang,Jing Li,Hongyu Chen,Ming Zhao,Yuxuan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为MergeProbe的轻量级预测器，用于在训练初期预测低秩适配器（LoRA）的可合并性，从而避免因适配器合并后出现破坏性干扰而导致的资源浪费。通过分析前几轮训练中的低秩更新及其梯度对齐情况、对共享表示的扰动程度等信号，该方法能够提前判断适配器是否适合合并，并据此做出直接合并、重加权、剪枝或路由的决策。在包含数学、代码、科学、指令遵循和安全性的五个领域基准测试中，MergeProbe在平均和最差情况下的保留率均优于现有主流干扰感知合并基线，且部署开销远低于全任务路由方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前低秩适配器（LoRA）虽能低成本训练多个特定任务的适配器，但其合并效果通常需在完全训练并评估后才能发现，存在高成本与不可预测性问题。特别是某些在单独训练时表现良好的适配器，在合并后可能产生破坏性干扰，因此亟需一种能在早期预判适配器合并可行性的方法。

Method: 提出并实现一个名为MergeProbe的轻量级预测模型，基于训练初期的低秩更新与梯度对齐程度、对共享表示的扰动等关键信号，量化适配器的可合并性；利用这些信号进行成对或集合级别的保留率预测，并据此生成具体的合并策略（如直接合并、重加权、剪枝或路由）。

Result: 在MERGE-PEFT五领域基准上，MergeProbe在平均保留率和最差情况保留率方面均优于现有强干扰感知合并基线方法，同时显著降低部署复杂度，相比全任务路由方案具有更小的开销。

Conclusion: 该研究将LoRA适配器的合并从传统的后期工程决策转变为可预测的前瞻性测量问题，有效提升了多任务适配器系统的效率与可靠性。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) makes it cheap to train many domain- and task-specific language model adapters, but whether two adapters can be merged is usually discovered only after both have been fully trained and evaluated. This late feedback is costly: adapters that are strong in isolation can interfere destructively once their updates are combined. We ask whether this outcome can be anticipated. We formalize adapter mergeability as the degree to which an adapter preserves its single-task utility after merging, and show that it can be forecast from signals measured in the first few percent of training -- chiefly how the low-rank updates and their gradients align across tasks and how much they disturb shared representations. We package these signals into MergeProbe, a lightweight predictor that estimates pairwise and set-level retention and turns the estimate into a concrete decision: merge directly, reweight, prune, or route. On MERGE-PEFT, a five-domain benchmark spanning math, code, science, instruction following, and safety, MergeProbe attains the best average and worst-case retention among strong interference-aware merge baselines while adding far less deployment overhead than full task routing. This turns LoRA merging from a post-hoc engineering step into an anticipatory measurement problem.

### [191] [Displacement Is Not Direction: Evaluating Fidelity Metrics for Quantized LLM Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19558)
*Miloš Nikolić,Ali Hadi Zadeh,Enrique Torres Sanchez,Andreas Moshovos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KLD作为基准质量的低成本代理在多数情况下表现良好，但在接近基线的沉默区域失效，且对代码任务失败预测能力弱，跨模型路由效果差。其主要衡量的是与参考模型的差异量，而非方向性，导致在关键场景下可靠性下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估当前广泛使用的低代价代理指标（如KLD）在真实模型性能评估中的有效性，特别是在接近基线的敏感区域和复杂任务中的表现。

Method: 在Qwen3.6-35B-A3B和Devstral-Small-2-24B两个模型系列上，通过多组下游基准测试，系统比较KLD与实际基准得分的相关性，并分析不同聚合方式、困惑度形式、校准语料等变体的影响，结合结构分解揭示KLD的本质作用机制。

Result: KLD在全量模型中与基准得分强相关（Qwen: ρ=-0.72, Devstral: ρ=-0.86），但在接近基线的沉默区域相关性消失（Qwen: ρ=+0.00, Devstral: ρ=-0.24, p=0.36）。在单个提示层面，对代码任务失败预测能力弱，跨模型路由准确率仅42.3%-49.4%。结构分解显示KLD主要反映差异体积而非方向，且该体积在沉默区高度相关（Qwen: +0.94, Devstral: +0.55）。

Conclusion: KLD虽在整体上可作为基准质量的近似代理，但其在沉默区失效、对任务方向性不敏感，限制了其在精细评估与模型选择中的可靠性，应谨慎使用并结合其他指标进行综合判断。

Abstract: Fidelity metrics, such as per-token KL divergence (KLD) against a high-precision reference, are often used in practice as low-cost proxies for benchmark quality. We test this practice on a 28-quant cohort of Qwen3.6-35B-A3B and a 41-quant cohort of Devstral-Small-2-24B, evaluated across a suite of downstream benchmarks. We find that KLD is strongly correlated with benchmark score over the full cohort ($ρ=-0.72$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.86$ on Devstral, both with $p<0.001$). However, this relationship collapses to non-significance in the near-baseline silent zone ($ρ=+0.00$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.24$, $p=0.36$, on Devstral). This collapse persists across 14 measurement variants, including different KLD aggregations, perplexity formulations, top-1 agreement, calibration corpora, and context lengths. At the per-prompt level, KLD has only weak failure-prediction power on code, with failed-vs-passed geometric-mean ratios in $[1.08,1.22]$ across five models on LiveCodeBench, and fails as a cross-model router, achieving only $42.3\%-49.4\%$ accuracy on disagreement prompts. We trace the collapse to a structural decomposition: KLD primarily measures the volume of disagreement with the reference, with silent-zone composite $ρ=+0.94$ ($p<0.001$) on Qwen and $+0.55$ ($p=0.03$) on Devstral, while its relationship to the direction of those disagreements is weak and task-conditional.

### [192] [Understanding Key Features of Time Series Foundation Models from Epidemic Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19560)

Result: 专家混合模型（融合多个预训练预测器）在所有任务中表现最优，表明异质预训练表示具有互补性；数值Transformer模型表现稳健，预训练在长周期预测中带来显著增益，尤其当预训练域与流感动力学机制一致时；基于LLM的方法整体表现不佳；住院数据在特定情境下可提升预测性能，增强多时程预测的鲁棒性。

We address this gap through a systematic evaluation of regional influenza forecasting using influenza-like illness surveillance and influenza-associated hospitalization time series under both temporal and spatial generalization settings for 1-4-week-ahead prediction. We compare classical neural network architectures, numerical transformer-based models, pretrained time series foundation models, and LLM-based forecasting approaches. Across tasks, we demonstrate that a mixture-of-experts model that fuses multiple pretrained forecasters achieves the strongest overall performance, indicating that heterogeneous pretrained representations provide complementary predictive information. In contrast, LLM-based time series methods underperform relative to numerical forecasters in this setting. ### [193] [Advances in Scientific Machine Learning for Coupled Fluid Flow and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19562)
*Gabriel F. Barros,Rômulo M. Silva,Alvaro L. G. A. Coutinho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文综述了科学机器学习（SciML）在建模由不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程和标量输运方程控制的耦合流体流动与传输现象方面的最新进展。针对强非线性耦合和多尺度行为导致的高保真模拟计算成本高昂的问题，文章介绍了基于奇异值分解（如动态模态分解）的线性降阶方法以及基于神经网络的非线性方法（如物理信息神经网络PINNs和β-变分自编码器β-VAEs）。结合高性能计算策略（如自适应网格细化/粗化和科学浮点数据压缩），文章展示了两项新贡献：利用PINNs对浊流进行代理建模，以及使用β-VAEs从热流中提取解耦的非线性模态。通过锁交换流动和瑞利-贝纳德对流等典型基准案例，阐明了这些方法的数学与物理基础及计算实现。研究表明，SciML可在特定数据范围和建模假设下实现快速、准确的复杂耦合系统近似，并显著降低计算成本；而实时预测与不确定性量化等更广泛能力仍处于研究阶段，其可行性取决于具体问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高保真模拟在处理具有强非线性耦合和多尺度特性的流体流动与传输系统时计算成本极高，难以满足实时或大规模应用需求。因此需要发展高效且准确的替代模型以降低计算开销。

Method: 结合线性降阶方法（如动态模态分解）与非线性神经网络方法（如PINNs和β-VAEs），并集成高性能计算技术（如自适应网格细化/粗化和科学浮点数据压缩），构建高效的代理模型。针对具体物理场景（如浊流和热对流），采用数据驱动与物理约束相结合的方式进行建模与模式提取。

Result: 成功实现了对浊流和热对流系统的高效代理建模，能够捕捉关键非线性动力学特征；相比全阶模拟，显著降低了计算成本；提取出具有物理意义的解耦非线性模态，提升了模型可解释性。

Conclusion: 科学机器学习为复杂耦合流体系统的快速、高精度建模提供了有效途径，在特定条件下可大幅减少计算资源消耗；未来在实时预测与不确定性量化方面仍有待深入探索，其适用性依赖于具体问题特性。

Abstract: This chapter reviews recent advances in Scientific Machine Learning (SciML) for modeling coupled fluid flow and transport phenomena governed by the incompressible Navier-Stokes and scalar transport equations. Such systems, found in applications like turbidity currents and thermal convection, feature strong nonlinear coupling and multiscale behavior that make high-fidelity simulations computationally expensive. To address this, the chapter surveys state-of-the-art SciML methods for building efficient surrogate models, including linear reduced-order techniques based on Singular Value Decomposition (such as Dynamic Mode Decomposition) and nonlinear neural network approaches like Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) and $β$-Variational Autoencoders ($β$-VAEs). It first covers the authors' work combining these models with High Performance Computing strategies, including Adaptive Mesh Refinement/Coarsening (AMR/C) and scientific floating-point data compression. It then presents two new contributions: surrogate modeling of turbidity currents via PINNs, and the extraction of disentangled nonlinear modes from thermal flows using $β$-VAEs. Governing equations and representative benchmarks, including lock-exchange flows and Rayleigh-Bénard convection, illustrate these methodologies. The chapter is intentionally long, covering both the mathematical and physical foundations of coupled fluid flow and the computational aspects of state-of-the-art modeling. Overall, it demonstrates how SciML enables fast, accurate approximations of complex coupled systems within the specific data regimes and modeling assumptions considered, while substantially reducing computational cost relative to full-order simulations. Broader capabilities such as real-time prediction and uncertainty quantification remain active research directions whose feasibility depends strongly on the problem at hand.

### [194] [On the QUEST for Uncertainty Quantification via Highest Density Regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19569)
*Sam Goring,Tom Kuipers,Nicola Paoletti,David S. Watson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QUEST 是一种基于最高密度区域（highest density regions）的不确定性量化新方法，通过衡量分布支撑集上最可能子集的体积来表征不确定性。该方法在应对非条件期望目标时避免了传统点预测风险方法的反直觉结果，并满足一系列经过适配的不确定性量化公理，包括单调性和位置不变性。实验表明，其性能优于方差、微分熵等标准度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于严格评分规则的标量不确定性量化方法在目标统计量非条件期望时会产生反直觉结果，需要一种更稳健且符合实际需求的不确定性表征方式。

Method: 提出基于最高密度区域（α-置信区域）的不确定性度量框架，利用勒贝格测度集中于分布峰值的特性，结合鲁棒参数 α 来评估不确定性，实现对认知和随机不确定性的分离与量化。

Result: QUEST 满足适应性公理（如单调性、位置不变性），在选择性预测基准测试中表现优于方差、微分熵等常用指标，具有更强的理论一致性和实证有效性。

Conclusion: QUEST 提供了一种新颖且理论严谨的不确定性量化框架，能够更准确地刻画复杂分布下的不确定性，尤其适用于非期望目标的回归任务，为安全关键场景中的可靠决策提供支持。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is essential for reliable decision-making in safety-critical applications in probabilistic machine learning. For regression problems, dominant scalar UQ approaches - notably, those based on proper scoring rules - measure uncertainty via pointwise predictive risk. This can lead to counterintuitive results when the target statistic is not the conditional expectation. We propose an alternative framework, in which uncertainty is characterised by the volume of the most probable subset of a distribution's support. QUEST (Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions) is a novel approach to UQ based on the concentration of Lebesgue measure at a distribution's peak(s), evaluated at one or more values of a robustness parameter $α$. We establish connections between our measures and classical statistics from information theory and economics. We show that, unlike popular alternatives based on proper scoring rules, QUEST measures of epistemic and aleatoric uncertainty satisfy a set of axioms adapted from the UQ literature, including monotonicity under distributional spread and invariance to location shifts. Selective prediction benchmarks confirm that QUEST performs favourably against standard measures such as variance and differential entropy.

</details>

Existing applications of this notion largely follow a hypothesis-testing paradigm: an expert proposes a candidate high-level model and then evaluates if the low-level system implements it. We study the complementary problem of learning a high-level model directly from low-level measurements. Our contributions leverage hypotheses from low-rank causal discovery, and can be summarized as follows: (1) we show that observations generated by a low-rank graph induce latents that form a causal abstraction, (2) we provide identifiability results about these latents, and (3) we propose a practical objective to learn this high-level SCM.

### [197] [Comparing Linear Probes with Mahalanobis Cosine Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19603)

TL;DR: Summary generation failed

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Abstract: Linear probes are widely used in interpretability research and often compared by cosine similarity. The Mahalanobis cosine similarity (MCS) between two directions, which reweights the inner product by test data covariance, is a natural task-aware refinement. Ying et al. (2026) report that a probe's MCS to a reference probe trained on the out-of-distribution (OOD) data near-perfectly linearly predicts the probe's OOD AUROC (R^2 = 0.98). Here, we extend this empirical finding across models, layers, and concept domains, and prove this general phenomenon in closed form: For balanced classes whose projections are Gaussian, OOD AUROC and MCS to the reference probe are linear because both are sigmoid-shaped functions of the probe's signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) on the test data. The theory also predicts when this linearity fails, which we verify empirically. MCS offers a theoretically grounded and empirically effective alternative to Euclidean cosine similarity for comparing linear probes.

### [198] [Latent Confounded Causal Discovery via Lie Bracket Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19610)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出两种在潜在混杂因素下的因果发现算法，基于Kan-Do-Calculus（KDC）的范畴论与信息几何。通过观测与干预分布间的Radon-Nikodym导数构造局部因果向量场，其李括号不闭合产生可计算的Frobenius残差，作为可见不可积性的证据，指示潜在结构。第一算法BRIDGE结合干预密度引擎与几何筛选，识别非闭合对作为潜在障碍候选，减少图空间复杂度；第二算法SKFM谱分解学习干预场并暴露李空间终点，与BRIDGE协同。实验表明二者能有效发现含潜变量的因果模型，显著压缩可能DAG空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果发现方法在存在潜在混杂时性能下降，缺乏直接从干预流中推断潜结构的机制。本文旨在建立一种基于范畴论与微分几何的新范式，将潜在结构识别转化为可计算的几何残差分析。

Method: 利用KDC框架下左/右凯恩扩展分别建模干预与条件，通过观测-干预测度间的Radon-Nikodym导数构建局部因果向量场；计算其李括号残差以检测可见不可积性；设计BRIDGE算法进行高召回候选边筛选与降维；引入SKFM算法通过谱分解学习干预场并揭示李空间终点，实现几何引导的因果发现。

Result: BRIDGE和SKFM在多个实验中成功识别出含潜变量的因果结构，将原本超指数规模的可能DAG空间压缩多个数量级，验证了基于几何残差的因果发现新范式的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了因果发现的新范式：潜变量结构可通过干预诱导流的几何特性（如李括号残差）直接推断。该方法融合范畴论、信息几何与机器学习，为复杂系统中的因果推理提供了强有力的理论与算法基础。

Abstract: Recent work on Kan-Do-Calculus (KDC) has established that the boundary between passive observation and active intervention in causal inference is a category-theoretic bi-adjunction, with interventions modeled by left Kan extensions and conditioning by right Kan extensions. This paper introduces two causal discovery algorithms under latent confounding, building on the information-geometric and categorical consequences of KDC. In smooth statistical settings, Radon-Nikodym derivatives between observational and interventional measures induce local causal vector fields; failures of these fields to close under Lie brackets become computable Frobenius residuals, which we interpret as witnesses of failed visible integrability and possible latent or unmodeled structure. Our first algorithm, BRIDGE (Bracket Residuals for Interventional Discovery and Geometric Estimation), combines an interventional density or Radon-Nikodym-ratio engine with a geometric screen that proposes a high-recall family of admissible arrows, identifies non-closing visible pairs as latent-obstruction candidates, and passes the reduced family to downstream score-based or differentiable discovery routines. The second algorithmic contribution, Spectral Kan-Do Flow Matching (SKFM), learns amortized intervention fields and factors latent curvature spectrally, exposing the direct Lie-space endpoint toward which BRIDGE points. A detailed set of experiments show that both algorithms are capable of discovering causal models with latent confounders while collapsing the super-exponential space of possible DAGs by many orders of magnitude. This paper introduces a new paradigm in causal discovery, where latent structure is inferred directly from the geometry of intervention-induced flows.

One promising domain is plant physiology, where measured responses often arise from multiple interacting processes whose exact separation remains difficult even with manual intervention. Here, we formulate limitation-state identification along A-Ci curves as a graph-based node classification problem, with curve points as nodes. The best-performing configuration, SEAGAN (domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes), integrates process-aware node features, edge attributes, kNN connectivity, and graph attention with weighted cross-entropy loss, achieving an F1-score of 0.857 and an accuracy of 0.882. Abstract: Math and science reasoning benchmarks rely on pass@k, the fraction of sampled chains that reach gold, as the canonical per-example difficulty signal. The same signal drives RL with verifiable rewards, math data curation, synthetic curricula, and verifier training. We show this proxy has a persistent blind spot on its hardest stratum: on the eight free-form math cells we test (GSM8K and MATH across four open-weight models), 10.3-22.9% of the examples that no sampling seed solves in six tries are instead solved at matched compute by a six-chain deterministic regime. These are greedy decoding plus five cheap residual-stream perturbations applied via activation grafting, while greedy alone solves at most 6% on these math cells. Recovery scales with the additional budget, across perturbations whose mechanistic distinctness we verify across all twelve cells (cross-kind fix-set Jaccard <= 0.47 in every setup). Activation grafting is used as an intervention on internal representations, not a decoding method; we use it purely as a diagnostic and diversification tool, and our recovered items show that the pass@k= 0 % stratum is structurally identifiable in the residual stream rather than that the unmodified model reaches them under ordinary inference.

*Masih Eskandar,Miquel Sirera Perelló,Stratis Ioannidis,Jennifer Dy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LOKI 是一种用于终身知识编辑的新方法，通过基于希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则的动态层选择和将梯度更新投影到模型权重的零空间，解决了现有方法在固定层修改、缺乏灵活性及需要访问历史知识等问题。该方法无需先前知识即可实现高效更新，并在多项实验中表现出色，平均准确率最高提升14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有终身知识编辑方法存在固定层修改导致灵活性不足、易引发灾难性遗忘，且需访问历史知识和复杂预处理的问题，限制了其在实际场景中的应用。

Method: LOKI 采用基于希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则的动态层选择机制，结合梯度更新投影到模型权重零空间的技术，避免对历史知识的依赖，实现更灵活、高效的模型更新。

Result: 在多种实验设置下，LOKI 表现优于现有方法，平均准确率最高提升14%，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: LOKI 通过动态层选择和零空间梯度投影，实现了无需历史数据访问的高效、灵活的知识编辑，显著缓解了灾难性遗忘问题，为语言模型的持续学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Lifelong knowledge editing aims to efficiently and sequentially update language models over time, as new knowledge becomes available or when the model makes mistakes, while preserving acceptable performance on past knowledge. One unresolved challenge is that existing methods modify a fixed set of layers for all new knowledge samples, reducing flexibility and increasing catastrophic forgetting. Another is requiring access to previous knowledge and extensive pre-processing to obtain data statistics. To address these challenges, we introduce LOKI, a novel approach that uses dynamic layer selection based on the Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion and projects gradient updates onto the null-space of the model weights, bypassing the requirement for previous knowledge access. We show that LOKI achieves superior performance to existing approaches across a wide variety of experiments, achieving up to a 14\% improvement in average accuracy.

</details>


### [204] [Multi-Granular Attention-Driven Reinforcement Learning Framework for Web Intelligent Enhancement Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19690)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习、深度学习和强化学习模型在不断演化的网络环境中面临语义理解能力弱、适应性差和可扩展性不足的问题，难以有效支持个性化、上下文感知的智能服务。

Method: 整合语义图建模、注意力机制和自适应多智能体强化学习；将异构网络数据预处理为统一特征表示，构建动态语义图，使用注意力增强的图嵌入捕捉上下文依赖，基于注意力感知的状态进行个性化动作优化，并通过在线反馈实时更新图结构与策略。

Result: 在准确率方面达到80%，显著优于现有方法，在个性化推荐、导航优化和服务自适应等任务中表现出更强的性能和适应性。

Conclusion: MGAR-WIES通过多粒度注意力与自适应强化学习的有效结合，实现了对动态异构网络数据的高效语义理解与实时个性化服务优化，具备良好的可扩展性与实用性，为下一代网络智能系统提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: From the past few years, web intelligent enhancement systems increasingly rely on heterogeneous and dynamic web data to deliver personalized, context-aware services. However, traditional machine learning, deep learning, and reinforcement learning models often struggle with semantic understanding, adaptability, and scalability in continuously evolving web environments. In this research, a Multi-Granular Attention-based Reinforcement Web Intelligent Enhancement System (MGAR-WIES) is proposed to address the challenges by integrating semantic graph modeling, attention mechanisms, and adaptive reinforcement learning. Initially, heterogeneous web data comprising structured, semi-structured and unstructured sources are collected and preprocessed for generating unified feature representations. These representations are transformed into a dynamic semantic graph, where entities and their relationships are modeled by using graph embeddings enhanced by attention mechanisms for capturing both local relevance and global contextual dependencies. Subsequently, an adaptive multi-agent reinforcement learning strategy leverages the attention-aware semantic states to optimize personalized web actions like content recommendation, navigation optimization, and service adaptation. Finally, the continuous online feedback is further integrated to update graph representations and learning policies in real time by ensuring sustained adaptability and performance. The proposed MGAR-WIES acheived better results in terms of accuracy (80%) when compared with existing approaches.

### [205] [Efficiently Representing Algorithms With Chain-of-Thought Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19697)
*Yanhong Li,Anej Svete,Ashish Sabharwal,William Merrill*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了链式思维（CoT）变换器是否能高效模拟Word RAM算法。研究表明，尽管传统的图灵机模拟存在二次复杂度开销，但CoT变换器在三种设置下（有限精度、连续推理和混合架构）均可实现对任意Word RAM算法的高效模拟，仅需多项式对数级别的额外开销，甚至在特定条件下可降至log-square或对数级别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论表明CoT变换器可模拟图灵机，具备通用计算能力，但图灵机模型不便于实际算法设计与分析。相比之下，Word RAM模型更贴近实际算法效率，因此问题在于CoT变换器能否高效模拟Word RAM算法，如快速排序或Dijkstra算法。

Method: 通过构建三类不同的CoT变换器模型：1）有限精度、多项式宽度且具有右端唯一硬注意力的变换器；2）连续推理的CoT模型（以向量形式进行思考）；3）基于线性RNN层的混合架构。在这些设定下，证明了它们能够模拟任意Word RAM算法，且仅引入多对数级开销。

Result: CoT变换器可以高效模拟任意Word RAM算法，其时间开销为多对数级别，当指令集平坦且无乘法时，开销可进一步降低至log-square或对数级别。这显著优于已知的图灵机模拟方式（需二次开销）。

Conclusion: CoT变换器不仅具备通用计算能力，还能高效模拟现实中的高效算法，其性能瓶颈远小于传统图灵机模拟，表明其在实际推理任务中具有巨大潜力。

Abstract: The increasing popularity of \emph{reasoning} models -- language models that output a series of reasoning or thought tokens before producing an answer -- is justified, in part, by theoretical results showing that chain-of-thought (CoT) transformers can simulate Turing machines, and thus perform arbitrary computation. However, the Turing machine, while suitable for complexity-theoretic analysis, is not convenient, intuitive, or efficient for discussing algorithms. Algorithms are typically designed and analyzed at a higher level of abstraction, captured by the \emph{Word RAM} model with random-access memory and unit-cost operations on $\bigO(\log n)$-bit words. As a result, Word RAM algorithms can be substantially more efficient than their Turing machine counterparts, raising the question: \emph{Can CoT transformers efficiently simulate Word RAM algorithms?} For instance, can they sort $n$ items in $\bigO(n \log n)$ steps or run Dijkstra's algorithm in $\bigO(E + V \log V)$ steps? We answer affirmatively, up to poly-logarithmic overhead. We first establish this for finite-precision transformers with poly-logarithmic width and rightmost unique hard attention, then strengthen the result to two more practical settings with finite width and log-precision: \emph{continuous} CoT, where reasoning takes the form of vectors rather than tokens, and a \emph{hybrid} architecture in which transformer layers sit atop a recurrent (linear RNN) layer. In all three cases, we find that CoT \emph{can} efficiently simulate any Word RAM algorithm with only a poly-logarithmic overhead in $n$. This overhead reduces to log-square when the Word RAM has a ``flat'' instruction set, and only logarithmic for multiplication-free flat instructions -- in stark contrast to known CoT simulations of Turing machines, which require quadratic overhead over Word RAM.

</details>


### [206] [Efficient Neural Network Model Selection for Few-Class Application Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19712)
*Bryan Bo Cao,Abhinav Sharma,Lawrence O'Gorman,Michael Coss,Shubham Jain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于数据属性的分类难度度量方法，用于高效选择少类场景下的神经网络模型。该方法显著提升了模型选择效率（快6至29倍），并可在保持性能的前提下，使模型体积缩小达42%，适用于移动机器人、无人机和物联网等资源受限场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注高性能神经网络的开发与评估，但较少考虑实际应用中常见的少类数据集特性对模型选择的影响。在真实世界中，许多任务仅涉及少量类别（如少于10类），而传统模型选择方法在此类场景下效果不佳。因此，需要一种更高效、适应性强的模型选择机制。

Method: 提出一种名为“少类独特性”（few-class distinctiveness）的分类难度度量方法，基于数据侧属性构建指标，用于快速评估和比较不同模型在少类数据上的表现，避免重复训练与测试。

Result: 该方法可实现模型与数据集比较速度提升6至29倍；在多个资源受限场景中，实现了比现有最小模型更小的模型规模，同时保持相近甚至更优的性能，例如在移动机器人任务中模型比YOLOv5-nano小42%。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于数据特性的分类难度度量，能够有效提升少类场景下的模型选择效率，为边缘设备上的轻量化模型部署提供实用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: While much effort has focused on developing and benchmarking high-performance neural networks, less attention has been given to how dataset properties, known to practitioners, can guide efficient model selection. Neural models are typically evaluated on datasets with thousands of classes, yet many real-world applications involve fewer than ten. To address this understudied but common setting, we develop a measure of classification difficulty based on data-side properties and show how it enables more efficient model selection for few-class datasets, where traditional approaches are less effective. We term this phenomenon "few-class distinctiveness". Our metric allows comparison of models and datasets 6 to 29$\times$ faster than repeated training and testing. Leveraging this insight, we extend scaled model families below the smallest published models, achieving greater efficiency at similar accuracy, for example models up to 42% smaller than YOLOv5-nano for a mobile robot task. Targeting resource-constrained applications, we demonstrate few-class model selection across mobile robot, drone, and IoT scenarios, highlighting practical gains in efficiency without sacrificing performance.

Abstract: In challenging real-world reinforcement learning applications, communication delays or sensor failures often cause frame dropping, in which the agent cannot receive the dropped states and associated rewards. Although DeFog can mitigate performance degradation in frame-dropping environments, since DeFog is an offline learning method, it struggles to effectively generalize to novel states not adequately represented in the training dataset. In this study, we propose OnDeFog, which integrates the mechanisms in DeFog with the online decision transformer (ODT), an online reinforcement learning method that learns policies through direct environmental interaction. Comprehensive experimental evaluation demonstrates that our proposed OnDeFog achieves superior performance compared to ODT in environments characterized by high dropping frame rate and outperforms DeFog on datasets containing a large amount of low-reward data.

### [208] [Federated Bilevel Performative Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19734)
*Liangxin Qian,Chang Liu,Xuanyu Cao,Jun Zhao,Kwok-Yan Lam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究联邦双层绩效预测问题，考虑客户端数据分布随决策变化的动态情形，提出联邦双层绩效稳定（FBPS）点，并给出其存在性和唯一性的充分条件。提出两种联邦算法：FBi-RRM（线性收敛）和FBi-SGD（通信高效，基于联邦超梯度估计，小敏感度下收敛）。实验验证了稳定性阈值预测，且在元学习和非凸神经网络场景中优于非绩效基线，展现出良好的实际效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦双层优化方法假设客户端数据分布固定，但现实中部署决策会改变客户端行为与数据收集，导致决策依赖的分布漂移。为应对这一挑战，需在联邦设置下建模和解决决策依赖的分布变化问题。

Method: 提出联邦双层绩效稳定（FBPS）点的概念，基于解耦风险视角建模；设计两类算法：FBi-RRM（基于收缩条件的确定性方法）和FBi-SGD（基于联邦超梯度估计的随机方法），分别保证线性收敛和渐进收敛。

Result: 理论证明了FBPS点的存在性与唯一性；实验表明所提方法能有效捕捉性能稳定性阈值，在战略回归、元策略分类及CNN分类任务中均实现比非绩效基线更优的元泛化能力，适用于非凸神经网络场景。

Conclusion: 本文首次在联邦双层优化框架下系统处理决策依赖的分布漂移问题，提出的模型与算法在理论上具有保障，在实践中显著提升元学习性能，为隐私保护下的动态分布式学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Federated bilevel optimization is widely used for nested learning problems across distributed clients, such as federated hyperparameter tuning and meta-learning under privacy and communication constraints. Most existing formulations assume fixed client data distributions, which can be violated by performativity, where deployed decisions reshape client behavior and data collection, inducing client-specific, decision-dependent distribution shift. We study federated bilevel performative prediction, where both upper-level (UL) and lower-level (LL) objectives are evaluated under client-dependent, decision-dependent distributions. We formalize the federated bilevel performatively stable (FBPS) point under a decoupled-risk perspective and provide sufficient conditions for its existence and uniqueness. We then develop two federated methods to compute the FBPS solution: FBi-RRM, which converges linearly under a contraction condition, and FBi-SGD, a communication-efficient stochastic method based on federated hypergradient estimation with convergence guarantees under diminishing step sizes when sensitivities are sufficiently small. Experiments on strategic regression and meta strategic classification validate the predicted stability thresholds and demonstrate improved meta-generalization over non-performative baselines, and CNN-based classification further demonstrates the practical effectiveness of the proposed methods in nonconvex neural network settings.

### [209] [Manifold Bandits: Bayesian Curriculum Learning over the Latent Geometry of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19750)
*Darrien McKenzie,Nicklas Hansen,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为贝叶斯流形课程（BMC）的结构感知框架，将问题采样建模为具有内生非平稳性的流形结构强化学习问题，通过层次化任务树与贝叶斯学习指导采样，克服传统方法仅关注难度而忽略任务空间结构的局限。实验表明，采样策略在效率、多样性与评估相关性之间存在显著权衡，单纯优先高难度问题不足以提升下游性能，强调需引入结构与类型感知机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自适应课程学习方法将问题选择视为独立臂的多臂赌博机问题，忽视了任务空间的结构性和异质性，导致训练效率受限。因此需要更精细地建模问题间的内在关联及其对学习信号演化的影响。

Method: 提出贝叶斯流形课程（BMC）框架，将问题组织成层次化任务树，利用贝叶斯学习动态优化采样策略，捕捉任务在模型隐空间中的流形结构及演化特性。

Result: 不同采样策略在生产力（学习信号）、多样性（任务流形覆盖）和实用性（评估相关性）之间呈现显著权衡；仅以难度为导向的策略无法实现最优下游性能，证明结构感知与类型意识的重要性。

Conclusion: 问题采样应超越单一难度优先原则，结合任务空间的结构特征与演化规律，通过结构感知机制可显著提升大语言模型的推理能力训练效率与效果。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is a central approach for improving reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs), where training efficiency depends critically on how problems are sampled during optimization. Existing adaptive curriculum learning methods typically prioritize prompts of intermediate difficulty, treating problem selection as a standard bandit problem with independent arms and overlooking the structured, heterogeneous nature of the task space. In this work, we frame problem sampling as a manifold-structured bandit problem with endogenous non-stationarity: problems are related through the model's latent representation space, and sampling decisions can steer how learning signals evolve across that space. To operationalize this perspective, we introduce Bayesian Manifold Curriculum (BMC), a structure-aware framework that organizes problems into a hierarchical task tree and applies Bayesian learning to guide sampling. Empirically, we find that different sampling strategies induce non-trivial tradeoffs between productivity (learning signal), diversity (coverage of the task manifold), and utility (evaluation relevance). These results show that prioritizing difficulty alone is insufficient for strong downstream performance, highlighting the importance of incorporating structure and type-awareness into problem sampling.

### [210] [Learning universal approximations for partial differential equations with Physics-Informed Broad Learning System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19754)
*Zhiwen Yu,Derong Yang,Liujian Zhang,Kaixiang Yang,Peilin Zhan,Jianmin Lv,Jane You,C. L. Philip Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为物理信息广义学习系统（PIBLS）的新框架，用于高效求解偏微分方程（PDEs）。该方法摒弃反向传播，通过直接最小二乘优化求解，显著提升速度与稳定性。针对非线性PDEs进行了算法改进，并提供了普适逼近性质的严格数学证明。实验表明，PIBLS比传统PINNs快1到3个数量级，同时精度更高，适用于实时模拟和设计优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解方法计算成本高且依赖网格，而现有PINNs存在收敛慢和优化不稳定的缺陷，亟需一种高效、稳定且无需网格的替代方案。

Method: 将PDE求解重构为无反向传播的直接最小二乘优化问题，利用广义学习系统实现快速求解，并对非线性情形进行算法优化，同时提供理论保证。

Result: 在各类线性和非线性PDE测试中，PIBLS相比传统PINNs在速度上提升1-3个数量级，同时保持或超越其精度，表现出卓越的效率与准确性。

Conclusion: PIBLS提供了一种计算高效的科学机器学习新范式，可作为实时仿真与设计优化任务的实用高速替代方案。

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) play a central role in modeling complex physical, biological, and engineering systems. While traditional numerical solvers are robust, they often incur prohibitive computational costs due to mesh dependencies, whereas recent Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) offer a mesh-free alternative but frequently suffer from slow convergence and optimization instability. To bridge this gap, this article proposes the Physics-Informed Broad Learning System (PIBLS), a novel backpropagation-free framework that reformulates PDE solving as a direct least-squares optimization. We improved an algorithm within this framework to handle nonlinear PDEs efficiently and provide a rigorous mathematical proof establishing the universal approximation property of PIBLS for these equations. Experiments on linear and nonlinear PDEs demonstrate that PIBLS is one to three orders of magnitude faster than conventional PINNs while achieving significantly higher solution accuracy. This framework provides a computationally efficient paradigm for scientific machine learning, offering a practical, high-speed alternative for real-time simulation and design optimization tasks.

### [211] [An Information Theoretic Framework for Graph Novelty Generation via Latent Mixture Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19770)
*Itsuki Nakagawa,Kenji Yamanishi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于信息论的图新颖性生成框架，通过在潜在空间中建模数据分布并利用有限混合模型生成新颖且结构一致的样本。新颖性通过要求生成样本无法被现有混合成分良好解释来强制实现，而可靠性则依据最小描述长度（MDL）原则约束其对整体混合结构的影响。理论分析表明，在适当阈值下，误分类非新颖或不可靠样本的概率以明确速率收敛至零。实验在合成和基准图数据集上验证了该方法能实现可量化的风险控制下的合理新颖性生成。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图数据生成方法难以在保持全局结构一致性的同时生成真正新颖的数据，且缺乏对生成数据新颖性和可靠性的量化评估机制。因此需要一种能够形式化定义新颖性与可靠性，并在理论上保证生成质量的框架。

Method: 将数据嵌入潜在空间，使用有限混合模型建模潜在分布；通过描述长度概念定义新颖性（生成样本对所有现有组件解释差）与可靠性（对整体混合结构影响小），并在最小描述长度（MDL）框架下进行优化生成。

Result: 理论分析证明了在合适阈值下，误判非新颖或不可靠样本的概率可快速收敛至零；实验结果显示该方法在合成与真实图数据集上均能有效生成结构一致且具有可量化风险的新颖图数据。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架为图数据的新颖性生成提供了理论保障与实践路径，能够在控制风险的前提下生成高质量、结构一致的新颖图数据，适用于需要安全、可解释生成的应用场景。

Abstract: We propose an information-theoretic framework for graph novelty generation, which aims to generate data that are distinct from existing patterns while preserving global structural consistency. Our approach embeds data into a latent space, models the latent distribution using finite mixture models, and generates novel samples by imposing explicit novelty and reliability conditions formulated in terms of description length. Specifically, novelty is enforced by requiring generated samples to be poorly explained by all existing mixture components, while reliability constrains their impact on the overall mixture structure under the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that, with appropriate threshold choices, the probabilities of misclassifying non-novel or unreliable samples converge to zero with explicit rates. Experiments on synthetic and benchmark graph datasets demonstrate that the proposed method enables principled novelty generation with quantifiable risk.

### [212] [Flow Map Denoisers: Traversing the Distortion-Perception Plane for Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19802)
*Nicolas Zilberstein,Morteza Mardani,Santiago Segarra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于流映射模型的新方法，通过调节一个称为'lookahead parameter'（前瞻参数）t，能够在图像恢复中的失真与感知质量之间连续控制，无需额外的配对数据、辅助模型或超参数调优。该方法在高斯目标下可精确实现最优失真-感知前沿，在自然图像上也表现出类似效果，并能扩展到各类逆问题中，同时保持良好的数据一致性与感知质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像恢复方法在最小化误差和最大化感知质量之间存在根本权衡：前者导致模糊重建，后者产生过于锐利但不忠实的图像。现有方法通常只能固定于某一点，或依赖复杂的监督、辅助模型或调参来切换不同操作点，难以灵活适应多样的需求。本文旨在解决这一灵活性与通用性不足的问题。

Method: 提出使用流映射模型（flow map models），其作为流匹配的一种少步采样扩展，学习平均场。该模型隐式定义了一个一参数族去噪器，其中前瞻参数 t 可连续调节从最小均方误差（MMSE）到感知优化之间的平衡。在插件式求解框架中，该机制可推广至一般逆问题，控制感知对齐与数据一致性的权衡。

Result: 在高斯分布目标下，理论证明改变 t 可精确覆盖最优失真-感知前沿；在自然图像上，实验验证了类似行为。在 CelebA（128×128）和 AFHQ（256×256）数据集上的多种线性和非线性逆任务中，单个训练好的流映射模型即可达到甚至超越专门针对极端情况设计的基线方法的性能。

Conclusion: 流映射模型通过单一参数 t 实现了图像恢复中失真与感知质量的连续调控，无需额外训练或调参，显著提升了方法的灵活性与实用性，为通用图像修复提供了新范式。

Abstract: Image restoration faces a fundamental tradeoff: methods that minimize error produce blurry reconstructions, while those that maximize perceptual quality yield sharp but less faithful images. Existing approaches either commit to a single operating point on this distortion perception (DP) frontier or require paired-data supervision, auxiliary models, or hyperparameter tuning of the sampler to access different points. We show that flow map models, a recent extension of flow matching for few-step sampling that learns an average field, implicitly define a one-parameter family of denoisers that continuously spans the DP frontier. The lookahead parameter t acts as a control knob between the MMSE and perceptual regimes. For Gaussian targets, we prove that varying t exactly recovers the optimal DP frontier; for natural images, we observe similar behavior empirically. Within a Plug-and-Play solver, the same mechanism extends to general inverse problems, where it controls a tradeoff between perceptual alignment and data consistency. Despite the lack of exact optimality guarantees in this setting, a single trained flow map spans the DP tradeoff, matching or exceeding specialized baselines at both extremes. Extensive experiments on CelebA ($128\times 128$) and AFHQ ($256\times 256$) across several linear and nonlinear inverse tasks validate our findings.

Method: 采用基于分位数的置信预测校准奖励模型的不确定性，并通过异方差方差分解对GRPO的优势进行重新加权，使模型能够识别并降低不可靠奖励的影响。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) aligns large language models by training reward models on preference data and optimizing policies to maximize predicted rewards. However, this pipeline faces two fundamental challenges: (1) reward models cannot signal when their predictions are unreliable, since they usually act as deterministic point estimators; and (2) modern group-based policy optimization can amplify unreliable reward signals, as exemplified by GRPO's uniform treatment of rewards during advantage computation. As policies explore increasingly diverse responses, these two limitations create a critical vulnerability: unreliable reward estimates may be granted disproportionate influence, triggering severe reward hacking. We propose Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling (UARM), which equips reward models with calibrated uncertainty via quantile-based conformal prediction and reweights GRPO advantages through heteroscedastic variance decomposition. We propose Adaptive Binning, a training-adaptive discretization pretext for tabular SSL that couples discretization to learning through a feature-wise coarse-to-fine curriculum. Motivated by the spectral bias of neural networks and the principles of curriculum learning, our method progressively refines discretization per feature upon plateau detection and selects representation-aware splits to jointly improve value-space concentration and representation-space coherence. A heterogeneity-aware objective unifies categorical reconstruction with ordinal supervision for numerical features, and experiments on public medical tabular datasets under unified evaluation protocols show consistent gains for linear probing and fine-tuning without dataset-specific discretization tuning. ### [218] [Global Convergence of Gradient Descent for Score Matching in Gaussian Mixtures via Reverse Fisher Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19876)
*Alexander Tyurin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究生成建模中的分数匹配问题，提出使用反向Fisher散度替代传统的前向Fisher散度作为优化目标。通过分析梯度下降在高斯混合模型上的行为，证明了反向散度具有更优的优化性质：在单个高斯教师分布下，无论初始值如何，都能实现全局收敛；在教师也为高斯混合模型时，在均值满足一定分离条件下，学生模型各成分可收敛至最近的教师成分，且整体分布以总变差距离收敛。证明依赖于一种新的基于李雅普诺夫函数的动态分析方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统前向Fisher散度在简单高斯混合模型中表现出依赖初始化的不良收敛行为，因此需要寻找更稳定的优化目标。

Method: 采用反向Fisher散度作为训练目标，通过构建新的李雅普诺夫函数分析梯度下降动力学，推导全局收敛性理论。

Result: 在教师为单高斯或高斯混合模型的情况下，反向Fisher散度下的梯度下降能实现从任意初始点出发的全局收敛，且学生分布以总变差距离收敛到教师分布。

Conclusion: 反向Fisher散度相比前向散度具有更优的优化景观，其梯度下降算法具备更强的收敛保证，适用于复杂生成模型的稳定训练。

Abstract: The score matching problem is a central training objective in modern generative modeling, diffusion models, fitting unnormalized statistical models, and inverse problems. A standard approach is to minimize the forward Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the teacher distribution. However, recent results show that even in simple Gaussian mixture model settings, this objective can lead to undesirable and initialization-dependent convergence behavior. In this paper, we study an alternative objective: the reverse Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the student distribution. We analyze gradient descent (GD) for fitting Gaussian mixture models and show that this change in the objective leads to significantly better optimization properties. First, when the teacher distribution is a single Gaussian and the student is a Gaussian mixture model with fixed weights and identity covariances, we prove the global convergence of GD from arbitrary initializations. Second, we extend the analysis to the case where the teacher is also a Gaussian mixture model and prove global convergence guarantees under a global random initialization scheme and a $\widetildeΩ(1)$-separation assumption on the target means. In particular, with high probability, each student component converges near its closest teacher component, and we provide conditions under which the student distribution converges in total variation distance. Our proofs rely on a new Lyapunov-based analysis of the gradient descent dynamics, showing that the reverse Fisher divergence has a much more favorable optimization landscape than the forward Fisher divergence.

### [219] [On the Oracle Complexity of Interpolation-Based Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19878)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作表明，经验风险最小化问题中损失函数在训练数据上的光滑性可被利用以改进梯度下降方法的查询复杂度。然而，如何有效利用这种数据域的光滑性仍需更高效的算法设计与理论分析。

Method: 提出PPI-GD方法，通过在数据域中等距点查询一阶优化器，构造梯度样本的多项式插值，并在适当大小的数据块上进行插值逼近全梯度。

Result: 在数据维度为样本数的多对数函数条件下，PPI-GD在强凸与非凸情形下均展现出优于多种标准梯度下降变体的查询复杂度，尤其在损失函数高度光滑时优势显著。同时，研究扩展了双三次样条的误差分析到d维张量积多项式插值，提供新的理论工具。

Conclusion: PPI-GD通过利用数据域的光滑性，显著降低了梯度查询复杂度，为高效优化提供了新思路；其插值分析技术亦具有潜在的理论价值。

Abstract: Recent work on first-order optimizers for empirical risk minimization (ERM) has suggested that smoothness of ERM loss functions in the training data, rather than in the optimization parameters, can be leveraged to improve the oracle complexity of gradient descent (GD) methods. In this paper, we propose an inexact gradient method, piecewise polynomial interpolation-based gradient descent (PPI-GD), which approximates the full gradient in each iteration by querying the first-order oracle at equidistant points in the data domain to construct polynomial interpolants of the resulting gradient samples over appropriately sized patches of the data domain. We analyze the oracle complexity of PPI-GD for strongly convex and non-convex loss functions when the data space dimension is bounded by a polylogarithmic function of the number of training samples, and find it to outperform several GD variants in key regimes when the loss function is sufficiently smooth. Furthermore, our analysis extends several techniques from the error analysis of bicubic spline interpolants to the setting of $d$-variate tensor product polynomial interpolants which may be of independent interest in interpolation analysis.

</details>


### [220] [Matching Markets meet Cumulative Prospect Theory: Towards Optimal and Adversarially Robust Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19883)
*Ananya Kunisetty,Avishek Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在竞争性双侧匹配市场中，基于人类中心决策模型的多智能体多臂赌博机问题。通过引入累积前景理论（CPT）来建模人类偏好，并使用α-霍尔德连续权重函数对行动进行非线性加权。分析了现有学习算法在CPT加权奖励下的表现，得到玩家最优后悔率为$\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}{\Delta}\right)^{2/\alpha})$。针对Δ依赖项次优的问题，通过巧妙选择探索期间的活跃臂集合，消除了主导项中对K的依赖，实现了当臂数K远大于玩家数N时的更优（最优）后悔界。此外，在对抗性市场下考虑奖励被污染的情况，提出了适用于总污染预算已知和未知情形的鲁棒算法，并在两种情况下均建立了对数级的玩家最优后悔界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多臂赌博机模型难以捕捉人类在决策中的非理性偏好；行为经济学与风险敏感机器学习中广泛使用的累积前景理论（CPT）提供了建模人类偏好的有效工具。然而，现有方法在双侧匹配市场与多智能体环境下的后悔分析尚不充分，尤其在高维、竞争性环境中存在性能瓶颈。因此，亟需设计适应人类偏好、具备鲁棒性的学习算法，以实现更优的后悔性能。

Method: 采用累积前景理论（CPT）作为风险敏感度量，引入α-霍尔德连续权重函数对奖励进行非线性扭曲；设计基于主动臂集选择的探索策略以降低对臂数K的依赖；在对抗性市场中，提出鲁棒算法，分别处理已知与未知污染预算的情形，结合在线优化与自适应机制提升稳定性与泛化能力。

Result: 在标准设置下，获得$\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}{\Delta}\right)^{2/\alpha})$的玩家最优后悔界；通过主动臂选择改进后，实现无K依赖的最优后悔界，特别适用于K远大于N的场景；在对抗性市场中，无论污染预算是否已知，均达到对数级玩家最优后悔界，证明了算法的鲁棒性与有效性。

Conclusion: 本文将累积前景理论融入多智能体双侧匹配市场的学习框架，显著提升了对人类偏好的建模能力，并通过改进探索策略与设计鲁棒算法，实现了在复杂竞争环境下更优的后悔性能。研究结果为人类中心决策系统中的智能体协作与竞争提供了理论支持与实用工具。

Abstract: We study a multi-agent multi-armed bandit problem in the competitive setup with two-sided matching markets under a human centric decision making model. To capture human preferences, we use cumulative prospect theory (CPT) that weighs the actions of the agent in a nonlinear fashion using a ($α$-Hölder continuous) weight function. CPT has been widely used in behavioral economics and risk sensitive machine learning to emulate human preferences. We analyze the state-of-the-art learning algorithm with CPT weight distorted rewards and obtain a player optimal regret of $\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}Δ\right)^{2/α})$, where $K$ denotes the number of arms, $T$ is the learning horizon, and $Δ$ represents (suitably defined) players' minimum preference gap. Noticing the dependence on $Δ$ to be sub-optimal, we further improve this regret by judiciously selecting the active set of arms during exploration, which removes the dependence on $K$ in the dominant term and achieves an improved (optimal) regret guarantees in the setting where the number of arms $K$ is significantly larger than the number of players $N$. In addition, we consider adversarial markets where the observed rewards of the agents may be corrupted. We propose and analyze algorithms for robust markets with CPT as risk sensitive measure in both settings where the total corruption budget is known and where it is unknown, and establish logarithmic player-optimal regret guarantees in both cases.

Abstract: Modeling long-sequence medical time series data, such as electrocardiograms (ECG), poses significant challenges due to high sampling rates, multichannel signal complexity, inherent noise, and limited labeled data. Structured state space models (S4) excel at long-sequence modeling, but existing S4 architectures fail to capture the unique characteristics of multichannel physiological waveforms. In this work, we propose SL-S4Wave, a self-supervised learning framework that combines contrastive learning with a tailored encoder built on structured state space models. The encoder incorporates multi-layer global convolution using multiscale subkernels, enabling the capture of both fine-grained local patterns and long-range temporal dependencies in noisy, high-resolution multichannel waveforms. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate that SL-S4Wave (1) consistently outperforms state-of-the-art supervised and self-supervised baselines in a challenging arrhythmia detection task, (2) achieves high performance with significantly fewer labeled examples, showcasing strong label efficiency, and (3) maintains robust performance on long waveform segments, highlighting its capacity to model complex temporal dynamics in long sequences that most existing approaches fail to efficiently model, and (4) transfers effectively to unseen arrhythmia types, underscoring its robust cross-domain generalization. Abstract: We study adversarial bandit optimization in which the loss functions may be non-convex and non-smooth. In each round, the learner selects an action and observes only the loss incurred at that action. The loss consists of an underlying convex and $β$-smooth component and an adversarial perturbation that may be chosen after observing the learner's action. The perturbations are subject to a global budget controlling their cumulative magnitude over time.
  This framework extends the globally budgeted, post-action perturbation model from underlying linear losses to general convex and $β$-smooth losses. For this broader class, we establish expected regret guarantees that explicitly characterize the effect of the perturbation budget.
  To establish these guarantees, we modify a standard bandit optimization algorithm and develop an analysis that controls the additional regret caused by the perturbations. In the absence of perturbations, our results reduce to regret guarantees for the standard bandit convex optimization setting with $β$-smooth losses.

### [223] [Score Approximation for Diffusion Models on Arbitrary Low-Dimensional Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19894)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本工作建立了适用于任意紧致支持集上分布的通用分数逼近理论，揭示了扩散模型在处理现实世界复杂数据结构时的强大能力，为其广泛应用提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: The remarkable success of score-based diffusion models has spurred significant efforts to establish their theoretical foundations. However, existing complexity bounds for score approximation rely heavily on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuous densities or smooth manifold supports, which are routinely violated by the singularities, sharp boundaries, and disjoint clusters inherent to real-world perceptual data. This work establishes a universal score approximation theorem that works for any distribution supported on any compact set of upper Minkowski dimension $d$. Using a novel discrete-mixture formulation, we prove that the score function can be approximated with a ReLU network whose complexity grows exponentially only with $d$, thus breaking the exponential curse of ambient dimensionality. Combined with existing theories on accurately solving the backward diffusion SDE for arbitrary compact distributions, our work shows that diffusion models readily adapt to irregular, non-smooth data structures, explaining their competence in real-world generative tasks.

### [224] [ADaPT: Token-Level Decoupling for Efficient Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19919)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ADaPT提出一种基于令牌级别的双过程框架，通过显式解耦效率与正确性信号来解决长思维链带来的高计算成本问题。它引入模式选择令牌，仅对这一令牌施加效率相关奖励，从而避免惩罚正确的长推理路径，同时在推理时可灵活调节效率与性能的权衡，实现平滑切换。实验表明，ADaPT显著降低推理开销，同时保持强推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在提升效率时往往牺牲推理能力，根源在于效率激励与正确性优化在序列层面耦合，导致长但正确的推理路径被隐式惩罚。

Method: 提出ADaPT框架，采用令牌级双过程机制，通过模式选择令牌控制快速与慢速推理，并仅对模式选择令牌施加效率奖励，实现效率与正确性的解耦训练；推理时通过调整该令牌生成概率，动态调节效率与性能平衡。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，ADaPT显著降低推理成本，同时保持优异的推理性能，支持在效率-性能之间平滑过渡。

Conclusion: ADaPT通过显式解耦效率与正确性信号，在不损害推理能力的前提下有效降低计算开销，为大模型推理提供了高效且灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Large reasoning models rely on long chain-of-thought to achieve strong performance, but applying such reasoning uniformly incurs high computational cost. Existing efficiency-oriented methods attempt to shorten or mix reasoning strategies, yet often degrade reasoning capability. We identify the root cause as sequence-level coupling between efficiency incentives and correctness optimization, which implicitly penalizes long but correct reasoning trajectories. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Dual-Process Thinking (ADaPT), a token-level dual-process framework that explicitly decouples efficiency and correctness signals during training. ADaPT introduces a mode-selection token to control fast and slow reasoning, applying efficiency-related rewards exclusively to this token to avoid penalizing correct long reasoning while encouraging efficiency when appropriate. Moreover, ADaPT enables precise and continuous control over the efficiency-performance trade-off at inference time: by adjusting the generation probability of the mode-selection token, a single trained model can smoothly move along the efficiency-performance Pareto frontier. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ADaPT significantly reduces inference cost while maintaining strong reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks.

*Dat H. Do,Rushi Shah,Duc V. Le,Dianbo Liu*
